<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Portal:Current events/December 2014</h1>

<p><b><a href="/wiki/December" title="December">December</a></b> <b><a href="/wiki/2014" title="2014">2014</a></b> was the twelfth and final month of that common year. The month, which began on a <a href="/wiki/Monday" title="Monday">Monday</a>, ended on a <a href="/wiki/Wednesday" title="Wednesday">Wednesday</a> after 31 days.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portal:Current_events"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Portal:Current events</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/December_2014&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Portal:Current events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>This is an <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events/How_to_archive_the_portal" title="Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal">archived version</a> of Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Current events Portal</a> from December 2014.</i></p>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background-color:transparent">
<tr>
<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div id="2014_December_1"></div>
<div id="2014_December_01"></div>
<table class="vevent" style="width:100%; margin:7px 0px; padding:2px; background-color:white; border:1px #cef2e0 solid;">
<tr>
<td>
<table cellspacing="0" class="plainlinks" style="background-color:#cef2e0" width="100%">
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 1, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-01</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_1&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_1&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iraqi_insurgency_(2011%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi insurgency (2011–present)">Iraqi insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Iraq" title="Prime Minister of Iraq">Prime Minister of Iraq</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Haidar_al-Abadi" title="Haidar al-Abadi">Haidar al-Abadi</a> promises a crackdown on corruption after an audit shows that there were 50,000 ghost soldiers in the <a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Army" title="Iraqi Army">Army</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-01/iraq-pm-says-graft-probe-found-50000-ghost-soldiers/5929524" rel="nofollow">(AFP via ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The Iraq Prime Minister fires 24 <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Interior_(Iraq)" title="Ministry of Interior (Iraq)">Interior Ministry</a> officials while the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_State_in_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State</a> kills at least 15 police officers near the border with <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/ap/article-2855878/UN-More-1-200-Iraqis-killed-November.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Naxalite-Maoist_insurgency" title="Naxalite-Maoist insurgency">Naxalite-Maoist insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maoist" title="Maoist">Maoist</a> rebels kill 14 <a href="/wiki/Central_Reserve_Police_Force" title="Central Reserve Police Force">Central Reserve Police Force</a> members in an ambush in <a href="/wiki/Chhattisgarh" title="Chhattisgarh">Chhattisgarh</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Central_India" title="Central India">Central India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-india-30278028" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist_insurgency_in_Nigeria" title="Islamist insurgency in Nigeria">Islamist insurgency in Nigeria</a>:
<ul>
<li>Dual <a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a> attacks in <a href="/wiki/Maiduguri" title="Maiduguri">Maiduguri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Damaturu" title="Damaturu">Damaturu</a> leave at least 77 dead, including 33 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Nigeria" title="Law enforcement in Nigeria">police</a>, 6 <a href="/wiki/Nigerian_Army" title="Nigerian Army">soldiers</a>, and 20 militants. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/dozens-reported-killed-in-attacks-on-nigerian-cities/" rel="nofollow">(CBS)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan</a>:
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomb" title="Suicide bomb">suicide bomb</a> kills at least nine, including two <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Afghanistan" title="Law enforcement in Afghanistan">policemen</a>, at a funeral for a tribal elder in <a href="/wiki/Baghlan_Province" title="Baghlan Province">Baghlan Province</a>, northern <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/asia/2014/12/suicide-blast-hits-afghanistan-funeral-baghlan-2014121764866837.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A search continues for 52 people missing from a <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> fishing vessel, the <i>Oriong-501</i>, that sank early in the morning in bad weather in the <a href="/wiki/Bering_Sea" title="Bering Sea">Bering Sea</a> off <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Chukotka_Autonomous_Okrug" title="Chukotka Autonomous Okrug">Chukotka Autonomous Okrug</a>. Eight people have been rescued including one person who subsequently died. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/reu-one-dead-dozens-missing-after-s-korean-vessel-sinks-off-russian-coast/2540761.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/World_AIDS_Day" title="World AIDS Day">World AIDS Day</a>:
<ul>
<li>Researchers claim that the <a href="/wiki/Pandemic" title="Pandemic">pandemic</a> has reached a <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Tipping_point" title="wiktionary:Tipping point">tipping point</a> where the number of people receiving treatment in a year was greater than the number of new cases. <a class="external text" href="http://m.whitehouse.gov/the-press-office/2014/11/29/presidential-proclamation-world-aids-day-2014" rel="nofollow">(U.S. Presidential Proclamation)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2014/12/01/health-aids-idINKCN0JF14320141201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> abandons its plans for the <a href="/wiki/South_Stream" title="South Stream">South Stream</a> pipeline to <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a> due to <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> objections instead looking at a pipeline to <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idAFKCN0JF2XE20141201" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Nations_World_Food_Program" title="United Nations World Food Program">United Nations World Food Program</a> suspends a food program for 1.7 million <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Syrian_people" title="Syrian people">Syrian</a> refugees after donor countries fail to meet their commitments. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/world/un-food-program-suspended-for-1-7-million-syrian-refugees-1.2856928" rel="nofollow">(AP via CBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> launches a new national defense facility in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> meant to monitor threats to national security in peacetime but take control of the country in wartime. <a class="external text" href="http://rt.com/news/210307-russia-national-defence-center/" rel="nofollow">(RT)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A group of 30 armed men raid <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea" title="Papua New Guinea">Papua New Guinea</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Lae_Nadzab_Airport" title="Lae Nadzab Airport">Lae Nadzab Airport</a> holding passengers hostage and ransacking offices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-01/armed-men-hold-passengers-captive-at-png-airport/5930840" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former Polish prime minister <a href="/wiki/Donald_Tusk" title="Donald Tusk">Donald Tusk</a> becomes the second full-time <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_European_Council" title="President of the European Council">President of the European Union</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://euobserver.com/institutional/126725" rel="nofollow">(<i>EUobserver</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Moldovan_parliamentary_election,_2014" title="Moldovan parliamentary election, 2014">Moldovan parliamentary election, 2014</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>'s pro-European parties begin consultations on forming a coalition as near-complete results show them gaining 54 seats in the 101-seat <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Moldova" title="Parliament of Moldova">parliament</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/moldova-coalition-talks-election/26719923.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Hong_Kong_protests" title="2014 Hong Kong protests">2014 Hong Kong protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Pro-democracy demonstrators and the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Police_Force" title="Hong Kong Police Force">Hong Kong Police Force</a> clash outside the headquarters of the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Hong_Kong" title="Government of Hong Kong">Government of Hong Kong</a>. Dozens of people are arrested. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/12/01/world/asia/protesters-storm-hong-kong-leaders-office-as-movement-flags.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2014/12/01/dozens-arrested-after-hong-kong-protesters-clash-with-police/" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Calgary_Stampeders" title="Calgary Stampeders">Calgary Stampeders</a> defeat the <a href="/wiki/Hamilton_Tiger-Cats" title="Hamilton Tiger-Cats">Hamilton Tiger-Cats</a> to win the <a href="/wiki/102nd_Grey_Cup" title="102nd Grey Cup">102nd Grey Cup</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.tsn.ca/" rel="nofollow">(<i>TSN</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 2, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-02</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_2&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_2&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflict and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2009%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2009–present)">War in Somalia</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Red_Cross" title="Red Cross">Red Cross</a> says that at least 36 people may be dead following an attack in <a href="/wiki/Mandera_County" title="Mandera County">Mandera County</a> in northeastern <a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a>. <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al-Shabaab</a> militants are believed to be responsible. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessweek.com/news/2014-12-02/kenya-red-cross-says-36-feared-dead-after-attack-in-northeast" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg via <i>Business Week</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/reuters/2014/12/02/world/africa/02reuters-kenya-attacks.html?partner=rss&amp;emc=rss&amp;smid=tw-nytimesworld&amp;_r=0" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War_spillover_in_Lebanon" title="Syrian Civil War spillover in Lebanon">Syrian Civil War spillover in Lebanon</a>
<ul>
<li>Unidentified gunmen kill 6 <a href="/wiki/Lebanese_Armed_Forces" title="Lebanese Armed Forces">Lebanese soldiers</a> near the eastern town of <a href="/wiki/Ras_Baalbek" title="Ras Baalbek">Ras Baalbek</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/middleeast/2014/12/lebanese-troops-killed-near-syrian-border-2014122193646646562.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_State_in_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanese</a> government arrests a wife and daughter of ISIL leader <a href="/wiki/Abu_Bakr_al-Baghdadi" title="Abu Bakr al-Baghdadi">Abu Bakr al-Baghdadi</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/storyline/isis-terror/isis-leader-abu-bakr-al-baghdadis-wife-son-detained-lebanon-n259551" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FBI" title="FBI">FBI</a> launches a probe into a massive hacking attack on <a href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures" title="Sony Pictures">Sony Pictures</a>, believing the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Politics_in_North_Korea" title="Politics in North Korea">leadership of North Korea</a> to be responsible. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/tech/2014/12/02/fbi-launches-probe-into-massive-sony-pictures-hack/" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A major Switzerland based commodities firm, <a href="/wiki/Trafigura" title="Trafigura">Trafigura</a>, played a "pivotal" role in the ability of the semi-autonomous <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kurd" title="Kurd">Kurdish</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> to export oil, exports that the central government in <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a> has prohibited. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/04/us-mideast-crisis-kurds-trafigura-exclus-idUSKCN0JI0MC20141204" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ebola_virus_epidemic_in_West_Africa" title="Ebola virus epidemic in West Africa">Ebola virus epidemic in West Africa</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a> quarantines the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tonkolili" title="Tonkolili">Tonkolili</a> district with more than half the country under lockdown and the official death toll in the country reaching 1,530 and roughly 7,109 infected. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-2858279/Sierra-Leone-widens-Ebola-quarantine.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> approves a plan by the <a href="/wiki/Christian_Council_of_Korea" title="Christian Council of Korea">Christian Council of Korea</a> to set up a large <a href="/wiki/Christmas_tree" title="Christmas tree">Christmas tree</a> near the border with <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> despite ongoing tensions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/ap/article-2856924/S-Koreans-light-new-frontline-Christmas-tree.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greek_people" title="Greek people">Greek</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anarchist" title="Anarchist">anarchists</a> burn a public transport bus and several cars during clashes with police in central <a href="/wiki/Athens" title="Athens">Athens</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/E/EU_GREECE_ANARCHIST_PROTEST?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT&amp;CTIME=2014-12-02-15-01-10" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> court sentences 185 people to death over their alleged involvement in a lethal attack on a police station on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.egyptindependent.com/news/egyptian-court-sentences-185-death-attack-police" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Egyptian Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Israeli prime minister <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> fires Justice Minister <a href="/wiki/Tzipi_Livni" title="Tzipi Livni">Tzipi Livni</a> and Finance Minister <a href="/wiki/Yair_Lapid" title="Yair Lapid">Yair Lapid</a> amid the imminent breakup of the government coalition and dissolution of the <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> ahead of <a href="/wiki/Israeli_legislative_election,_2015" title="Israeli legislative election, 2015">new elections</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesofisrael.com/netanyahu-fires-lapid-livni-from-ministerial-posts/#ixzz3KlGVXWkf" rel="nofollow">(Times of Israel)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Sweden_Democrats" title="Sweden Democrats">Sweden Democrats</a> decide to vote for the opposition's budget proposal, likely forcing the collapse of Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Stefan_L%C3%B6fven" title="Stefan Löfven">Stefan Löfven</a>'s new government that came to power in the <a href="/wiki/Swedish_general_election,_2014" title="Swedish general election, 2014">September elections</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Politics/wireStory/swedish-government-faces-crisis-budget-27305573" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Hong_Kong_protests" title="2014 Hong Kong protests">2014 Hong Kong protests</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C._Y._Leung" title="C. Y. Leung">C. Y. Leung</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Chief_Executive_of_Hong_Kong" title="Chief Executive of Hong Kong">Chief Executive of Hong Kong</a>, warns pro-democracy activists not to return to the streets after yesterday's clashes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30287965" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Ukraine" title="Parliament of Ukraine">Parliament of Ukraine</a> approves the formation of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Second_Yatsenyuk_Government" title="Second Yatsenyuk Government">new government</a> that includes three foreigners who have received <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_citizenship" title="Ukrainian citizenship">Ukrainian citizenship</a> just hours before the vote: Georgian-born <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Kvitashvili" title="Alexander Kvitashvili">Alexander Kvitashvili</a>, US-national <a href="/wiki/Natalie_Jaresko" title="Natalie Jaresko">Natalie Jaresko</a> and Lithuanian <a href="/wiki/Aivaras_Abromavi%C4%8Dius" title="Aivaras Abromavičius">Aivaras Abromavičius</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/europe/2014/12/ukraine-appoints-three-non-native-ministers-20141221954454451.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/ukraine-government-rebels-agree-cease-fire-27297823" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Foreign ministers from members of <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> attend a summit in <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> to discuss the <a href="/wiki/2014_pro-Russian_unrest_in_Ukraine" title="2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine">2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_State_in_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant</a> insurgency. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/video/2014-12/03/c_133829028.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Transparency_International" title="Transparency International">Transparency International</a> issues its 2014 <a href="/wiki/Corruption_Perceptions_Index" title="Corruption Perceptions Index">Corruption Perceptions Index</a> with <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a> achieving the highest rating and <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> tied with the lowest ranking. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/03/us-corruption-ranking-idUSKCN0JH09A20141203" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> police arrest a mix of mafia gangsters, corrupt politicians, and one former terrorist in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Rome_corruption_scandal" title="2014 Rome corruption scandal">corruption scandal</a> exploiting migrants and gipsies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/italy/11271882/Mafia-capital-Rome-hit-by-mobster-scandal.html" rel="nofollow">(Telegraph)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> parliament- the <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> votes to dissolve the government and hold <a href="/wiki/Israeli_legislative_election,_2015" title="Israeli legislative election, 2015">early election</a> on March 17. <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/news/national/.premium-1.629714#!" rel="nofollow">(Haaretz)</a></li>
<li>Less than three months after winning the <a href="/wiki/Swedish_general_election,_2014" title="Swedish general election, 2014">general election</a>, <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Sweden" title="Prime Minister of Sweden">Prime Minister of Sweden</a> <a href="/wiki/Stefan_L%C3%B6fven" title="Stefan Löfven">Stefan Löfven</a> calls a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Swedish_general_election,_2015" title="Swedish general election, 2015">snap general election</a> after parliament rejected his government's budget proposal. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-30306992" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> space agency, <a href="/wiki/JAXA" title="JAXA">JAXA</a>, launches the space explorer <a href="/wiki/Hayabusa_2" title="Hayabusa 2">Hayabusa 2</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Tanegashima_Space_Center" title="Tanegashima Space Center">Tanegashima Space Center</a> on a six-year roundtrip mission to the asteroid <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/(162173)_1999_JU3" title="(162173) 1999 JU3">(162173) 1999 JU3</a> to collect rock samples. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/A/AS_JAPAN_SPACE_EXPLORATION?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>Islamic insurgents kill three <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Russia" title="Law enforcement in Russia">state police</a> at a traffic circle before taking an empty school and a "press house" in <a href="/wiki/Grozny" title="Grozny">Grozny</a>. <li>An estimated 3000m³ of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crude_oil" title="Crude oil">crude oil</a> from a damaged <a href="/wiki/Trans-Israel_pipeline" title="Trans-Israel pipeline">pipeline</a> leak into a <a href="/wiki/National_parks_and_nature_reserves_of_Israel" title="National parks and nature reserves of Israel">nature reservation</a> in <a href="/wiki/Arabah" title="Arabah">Arava desert</a> in southern <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw.de/burst-oil-pipeline-floods-israeli-nature-reserve/a-18109654" rel="nofollow">(DW)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4599798,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a></li>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_Jammu_and_Kashmir" title="Insurgency in Jammu and Kashmir">Kashmir insurgency</a>:
<ul>
<li>An attack on a military camp leaves 11 <a href="/wiki/Indian_Army" title="Indian Army">Indian soldiers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_India" title="Law enforcement in India">police</a> dead near <a href="/wiki/Uri,_Jammu_and_Kashmir" title="Uri, Jammu and Kashmir">Uri</a>. Eight militants and two civilians are killed in that and concurrent attacks in the state capital, <a href="/wiki/Srinagar" title="Srinagar">Srinagar</a>, and a part of southern <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/idUSKCN0JJ0CA20141205?irpc=932" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Terrorism_in_Somalia" title="Terrorism in Somalia">Terrorism in Somalia</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomb" title="Suicide bomb">suicide bomb</a> attack kills at least 10 at a restaurant in <a href="/wiki/Baidoa" title="Baidoa">Baidoa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/africa/2014/12/deadly-suicide-attack-hits-somali-town-2014125181558189581.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A judge in the Netherlands declares <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> clothing company <a href="/wiki/Mexx" title="Mexx">Mexx</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bankrupt" title="Bankrupt">bankrupt</a>. The bankruptcy ruling affects over 300 stores worldwide, including 95 locations in <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/business/mexx-goes-bankrupt-affecting-95-canadian-stores-1.2861928?" rel="nofollow">(CBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Italian rescue crews discover 17 bodies in the hull of a migrant ship off Libya. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2014/12/05/reports-at-least-17-bodies-found-in-migrant-ship-off-libya-italy-insists-it/?intcmp=HPBucket" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International Relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/British_Museum" title="British Museum">British Museum</a> announces that it will loan one of the <a href="/wiki/Elgin_Marbles" title="Elgin Marbles">Elgin Marbles</a> in its collection, originally taken from <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>, to the <a href="/wiki/Hermitage_Museum" title="Hermitage Museum">Hermitage Museum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>. <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Greece" title="Prime Minister of Greece">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Antonis_Samaras" title="Antonis Samaras">Antonis Samaras</a> calls the move "a provocation to the Greek people." <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2014/12/05/world/europe/uk-elgin-marbles-russia/index.html?hpt=hp_c5" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and Crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>China's <a href="/wiki/Supreme_People%27s_Procuratorate" title="Supreme People's Procuratorate">Supreme People's Procuratorate</a> arrests former <a href="/wiki/Politburo_Standing_Committee_of_the_Communist_Party_of_China" title="Politburo Standing Committee of the Communist Party of China">Politburo Standing Committee</a> member <a href="/wiki/Zhou_Yongkang" title="Zhou Yongkang">Zhou Yongkang</a> on corruption charges and expels him from the <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="Communist Party of China">Communist Party of China</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-china-30352458" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bill_Cosby" title="Bill Cosby">Bill Cosby</a> files a counter-lawsuit against the woman who accused him of sexual assault, claiming she attempted to extort money from him. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-us-canada-30343324" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone_Magazine" title="Rolling Stone Magazine">Rolling Stone Magazine</a> issues a partial retraction on <a href="/wiki/Sabrina_Erdely#UVA_rape_reporting" title="Sabrina Erdely">Sabrina Erdely's "A Rape on Campus" story</a> after additional <a href="/wiki/Fact_checking" title="Fact checking">fact checking</a> identifies "discrepancies" in the account of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Virginia" title="University of Virginia">University of Virginia</a> young woman identified as "Jackie" who alleged that seven men raped her as she lay on broken glass during a party at U.Va.'s <a href="/wiki/Phi_Kappa_Psi" title="Phi Kappa Psi">Phi Kappa Psi</a> fraternity in 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rollingstone.com/culture/news/a-note-to-our-readers-20141205" rel="nofollow">(<i>Rolling Stone</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/blogs/erik-wemple/wp/2014/12/02/rolling-stone-whiffs-in-reporting-on-alleged-rape/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesdispatch.com/news/state-regional/rolling-stone-backs-off-its-u-va-rape-story/article_82f71500-0cd8-5ae5-9114-fd62d01f0995.html" rel="nofollow">(TimesDispatch)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and Technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Exploration_Flight_Test_1" title="Exploration Flight Test 1">The first flight test</a> of <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Orion_(spacecraft)" title="Orion (spacecraft)">Orion spacecraft</a> launches successfully at 7:05 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Standard_Time_(North_America)" title="Eastern Standard Time (North America)">EST</a> (12:05 UTC) and splashes down safely in the Pacific Ocean at 8:29 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Standard_Time" title="Pacific Standard Time">PST</a> (16:29 UTC). <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/05/tech/innovation/nasa-orion-launch/index.html?hpt=hp_t2" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<li><a href="/wiki/2014_hostage_rescue_operations_in_Yemen" title="2014 hostage rescue operations in Yemen">2014 hostage rescue operations in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>An American civilian and a South African civilian die during an attempt to rescue them by <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy_SEALs" title="United States Navy SEALs">U.S. Navy SEALs</a> in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. They were being held hostage by <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Arabian_Peninsula" title="Al-Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula">al-Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/06/world/meast/yemen-u-s-hostage-killed/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Iguala_mass_kidnapping" title="2014 Iguala mass kidnapping">2014 Iguala mass kidnapping</a>
<ul>
<li>Forensic specialists at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Innsbruck" title="University of Innsbruck">University of Innsbruck</a> confirm the identity of the first of the 43 missing students in <a href="/wiki/Guerrero" title="Guerrero">Guerrero</a>. The remains were located at a municipal dump in <a href="/wiki/Cocula,_Guerrero" title="Cocula, Guerrero">Cocula, Guerrero</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.eluniversal.com.mx/nacion-mexico/2014/reportan-a-padres-que-restos-de-cocula-son-de-normalista-1059936.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>El Universal)</i></a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Armed_Forces" title="Syrian Armed Forces">Syrian Army</a> repels an <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> offensive on the <a href="/wiki/Deir_ez-Zor" title="Deir ez-Zor">Deir ez-Zor</a> air base, resulting in at least 119 casualties total. <a class="external text" href="http://www.khaleejtimes.com/kt-article-display-1.asp?xfile=data/middleeast/2014/December/middleeast_December53.xml&amp;section=middleeast" rel="nofollow">(Khaleej Times)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Unidentified gunmen break into a prison and free an estimated 200 inmates in <a href="/wiki/Minna" title="Minna">Minna</a>, west-central <a href="/wiki/Niger_State" title="Niger State">Niger State</a> in <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/prison-break-frees-200-inmates-central-nigeria-n263331" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hagupit_(2014)" title="Typhoon Hagupit (2014)">Typhoon Hagupit (Ruby)</a>, a strong tropical cyclone, makes landfall hitting the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30356298" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<ul>
<li>Demonstrations continue for a third day in <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>, <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">Boston</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chicago" title="Chicago">Chicago</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">Cleveland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jacksonville,_Florida" title="Jacksonville, Florida">Jacksonville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Miami" title="Miami">Miami</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> where protesters perform "<a href="/wiki/Die-in" title="Die-in">die-ins</a>" over the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_of_Michael_Brown" title="Death of Michael Brown">deaths of Michael Brown</a> and <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Eric_Garner" title="Death of Eric Garner">Eric Garner</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://mobile.nytimes.com/2014/12/05/nyregion/protests-continue-after-grand-jury-decision-in-eric-garner-case.html?referrer=" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.boston.com/news/local/massachusetts/2014/12/04/protest-against-cops-killing-unarmed-black-men-underway-boston/0xxwtOjcbB0PAfx5Scdh9M/story.html" rel="nofollow">(Boston.com)</a></li>

New Horizons, launched on January 19, 2006, will begin distant observations on January 15, 2015, culminating with its July 14, 2015 closest approach flyby. <a class="external text" href="http://www.skyandtelescope.com/astronomy-news/new-horizons-awakens-12062014/" rel="nofollow">(Sky and Telescope)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/science/sciencenow/la-sci-sn-pluto-new-horizons-hibernation-nasa-20141205-story.html" rel="nofollow">(L.A. <ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Philippines_v._China" title="Philippines v. China">Philippines v. China</a></i>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> condemns the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> over the latter's "pressure" over the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a> despite the disadvantage of the <a href="/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Philippines" title="Armed Forces of the Philippines">Armed Forces of the Philippines</a> against China's <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Liberation_Army" title="People's Liberation Army">People's Liberation Army</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/news/asia/south-east-asia/story/china-denounces-the-philippines-its-pressure-over-sea-dispute-arbitr" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sunday Times</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://mobile.bloomberg.com/news/2014-12-07/china-rejects-arbitration-of-disputes-in-south-china-sea.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_administration" title="Obama administration">Obama administration</a> orders the transfer of six prisoners from <a href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_detention_camp" title="Guantanamo Bay detention camp">Guantanamo Bay detention camp</a> to <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>, the largest single group of detainees to be released in five years and the first to be resettled in South America. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/12/08/world/americas/us-transfers-6-guantanamo-detainees-to-uruguay.html?_r=0#" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Interior_(Saudi_Arabia)" title="Ministry of Interior (Saudi Arabia)">Saudi Interior Ministry</a> arrests 135 on terrorism offences, including dozens suspected of links to <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/middleeast/2014/12/saudi-arrests-135-people-terrorism-charges-2014127224758210316.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Chlorine" title="Chlorine">chlorine</a> gas leak injures 19 at the Chicago's 'Furfest', a <a href="/wiki/Furry_fandom" title="Furry fandom">Furry</a> <a href="/wiki/Furry_convention" title="Furry convention">convention</a>. Police say the act was <a href="/wiki/Chlorine#Use_as_a_weapon" title="Chlorine">intentional</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcchicago.com/news/local/Intentional-Chemical-Leak-at-Hyatt-Regency-285008481.html" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democrat</a> <a href="/wiki/Mary_Landrieu" title="Mary Landrieu">Mary Landrieu</a> loses her bid for a fourth <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate#term" title="United States Senate">term</a> representing <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> to <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> Congressman <a href="/wiki/Bill_Cassidy" title="Bill Cassidy">Bill Cassidy</a> in Saturday's <a href="/wiki/Two-round_system" title="Two-round system">runoff election</a>, increasing the GOP majority in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Senate" title="U.S. Senate">U.S. Senate</a> to 54 seats. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/2014/12/06/cassidy-landrieu-senate-runoff/20000201/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsweek.com/southern-democrats-senate-nearly-extinct-landrieu-loses-289897" rel="nofollow">(Newsweek)</a></li>

<dt>Business and economy</dt>

<li><a href="/wiki/Merck_%26_Co." title="Merck &amp; Co.">Merck</a> agrees to buy "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Antibiotic_resistance" title="Antibiotic resistance">superbug</a>"-fighter <a href="/wiki/Cubist_Pharmaceuticals" title="Cubist Pharmaceuticals">Cubist Pharmaceuticals</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_dollars" title="United States dollars">$</a>9.5 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxbusiness.com/industries/2014/12/08/merck-takes-aim-at-superbugs-with-5-billion-cubist-buy/" rel="nofollow">(FOX Business)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hagupit_(2014)" title="Typhoon Hagupit (2014)">Typhoon Hagupit</a>
<ul>
<li>The Philippine Red Cross estimates 27 people killed in <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Samar" title="Eastern Samar">Eastern Samar</a> province with 15 in <a href="/wiki/Borongan" title="Borongan">Borongan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/08/us-philippines-typhoon-idUSKBN0JM04420141208" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Trust)</a></li>

<li>A small plane crashes into a house in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/American_people" title="American people">American</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Gaithersburg,_Maryland" title="Gaithersburg, Maryland">Gaithersburg, Maryland</a> near <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> with 5 people dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.skynews.com.au/news/world/nthamerica/2014/12/09/us-mum--sons-die-as-plane-slams-into-home.html" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> seeks <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_dollars" title="United States dollars">$</a>16.4 billion to fund humanitarian assistance programs in 2015 with <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> the areas of greatest need. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/12/09/world/middleeast/un-seeks-164-billion-to-address-crises-in-2015.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_2014_%C3%9Cr%C3%BCmqi_attack" title="May 2014 Ürümqi attack">May 2014 Ürümqi attack</a>:
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Judicial_system_in_China" title="Judicial system in China">Chinese court</a> sentences eight people to death for their role in two deadly attacks in <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-2865134/Eight-sentenced-death-attacks-Chinas-Xinjiang-CCTV.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernard_Madoff" title="Bernard Madoff">Bernard Madoff</a> <a href="/wiki/Madoff_investment_scandal" title="Madoff investment scandal">Ponzi scheme</a>:
<ul>
<li>A U.S. District Judge sentences the back office director, Daniel Bonventre, to ten years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxbusiness.com/2014/12/08/former-madoff-back-office-director-gets-10-years/" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via FOX Business)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">US Supreme Court</a> rejects <a href="/wiki/BP" title="BP">BP</a>'s challenge to their <a href="/wiki/Deepwater_Horizon_oil_spill" title="Deepwater Horizon oil spill"><i>Deepwater Horizon</i> gulf oil spill</a> settlement. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxbusiness.com/industries/2014/12/08/scotus-rejects-bp-challenge-to-gulf-spill-settlement/" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via FOX Business)</a></li>
<li>United States President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> unveils new limits on <a href="/wiki/Racial_profiling" title="Racial profiling">racial profiling</a>. These new limits outlaw profiling based on race, gender, ethnicity, nationality, religion, or sexual orientation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/blogs/thetwo-way/2014/12/08/369388099/obama-administration-unveils-new-ban-on-racial-profiling" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset</a> votes to dissolve itself with <a href="/wiki/Israeli_legislative_election,_2015" title="Israeli legislative election, 2015">new elections</a> called for March 17. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/M/ML_ISRAEL_POLITICS?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 9, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-09</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_9&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_9&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_9&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Ansar_al-Sharia_(Yemen)" title="Ansar al-Sharia (Yemen)">Ansar al-Sharia</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomb" title="Suicide bomb">suicide bomb</a> attack kills seven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yemen_Army" title="Yemen Army">soldiers</a> at an army base in <a href="/wiki/Hadhramaut_Governorate" title="Hadhramaut Governorate">southern Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/09/world/meast/yemen-violence/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Three <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkish_Army" title="Turkish Army">Turkish Army</a> soldiers die by gunfire in the town of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ceylanpinar" title="Ceylanpinar">Ceylanpinar</a>. The local Turkish governor begins an investigation of whether the gunfire came from the <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> side of the border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-30389859" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Another bomb explodes (the previous was November 6, 2014) on a passenger bus, killing at least 11 people and injuring 21 in the southern <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> province of <a href="/wiki/Bukidnon" title="Bukidnon">Bukidnon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/world/2014-12/09/c_133843492.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda_in_the_Islamic_Maghreb" title="Al Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb">Al Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb</a> release Serge Lazarevic, a <a href="/wiki/French_people" title="French people">French hostage</a> seized three years ago in <a href="/wiki/Mali" title="Mali">Mali</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/12/10/world/europe/french-hostage-serge-lazarevic-released.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(NYTimes)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A court in <a href="/wiki/Lismore,_New_South_Wales" title="Lismore, New South Wales">Lismore, Australia</a>, convicts the former <a href="/wiki/National_Rugby_League" title="National Rugby League">National Rugby League</a> player <a href="/wiki/Craig_Field" title="Craig Field">Craig Field</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Manslaughter" title="Manslaughter">manslaughter</a> of Kelvin Kane outside the <a href="/wiki/Kingscliff,_New_South_Wales" title="Kingscliff, New South Wales">Kingscliff</a> Hotel in 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-09/ex-league-star-craig-field-guilty-of-manslaughter/5955040" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">US Supreme Court</a> rules 9–0 (Integrity Staffing Solutions, Inc. v. Busk) in favor of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amazon.com_Inc." title="Amazon.com Inc.">Amazon.com Inc.</a> that employees are not entitled to be paid for the time they spend undergoing security checks after their shifts. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/09/us-usa-court-workers-idUSKBN0JN1P820141209" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pirate_Bay" title="Pirate Bay">Pirate Bay</a> <a href="/wiki/Website" title="Website">website</a> goes offline after <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Sweden" title="Law enforcement in Sweden">Swedish police</a> seize its servers. <a class="external text" href="http://thenextweb.com/apps/2014/12/09/pirate-bay-offline-swedish-police-raid/" rel="nofollow">(The Next Web)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democrat</a>-controlled <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate_Select_Committee_on_Intelligence" title="United States Senate Select Committee on Intelligence">United States Senate Select Committee on Intelligence</a> releases a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_Intelligence_Committee_report_on_the_CIA%27s_interrogation_policies_post_September_11" title="Senate Intelligence Committee report on the CIA's interrogation policies post September 11">report</a> critical of the post-<a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">September 11</a> <a href="/wiki/Presidency_of_George_W._Bush" title="Presidency of George W. Bush">Bush Administration</a>-era <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CIA" title="CIA">CIA</a> interrogation techniques used to extract intelligence from captured <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a> operatives. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_Administration" title="Obama Administration">Obama Administration</a> places US embassies around the world on high alert. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-us-canada-30383924" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Hong_Kong_protests" title="2014 Hong Kong protests">2014 Hong Kong protests</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Police_Force" title="Hong Kong Police Force">Hong Kong Police Force</a> warn protesters that they have until Thursday to leave their protest camp in <a href="/wiki/Admiralty,_Hong_Kong" title="Admiralty, Hong Kong">Admiralty</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/hong-kong-democracy-protest-camp-shutdown-looms-27462495" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Nature_(journal)" title="Nature (journal)">Nature</a></i> publishes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Penn_State_University" title="Penn State University">Penn State University</a> findings of Ancient shells with 430,000-year-old engravings believed to be made by <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_erectus" title="Homo erectus">Homo erectus</a></i>, changing beliefs on artistic expression and tool use by ancestors of <i><a href="/wiki/Homo_sapiens" title="Homo sapiens">Homo sapiens</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Dutch_people" title="Dutch people">Dutch</a> <a href="/wiki/Anthropologist" title="Anthropologist">anthropologist</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eugene_Dubois" title="Eugene Dubois">Eugene Dubois</a> found the collection in <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a> in 1891 and Penn State discovered the markings in a museum in the city of <a href="/wiki/Leiden" title="Leiden">Leiden</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.watoday.com.au/technology/sci-tech/earliest-known-engravings-by-a-human-ancestor-found-on-a-clam-shell-20141209-122x8b.html" rel="nofollow">(WA Today)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 10, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-10</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_10&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_10&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_10&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The settlement minister of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_Authority" title="Palestinian Authority">Palestinian Authority</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ziad_Abu_Ein" title="Ziad Abu Ein">Ziad Abu Ein</a>, dies after a confrontation with <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> soldiers during a <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a> protest. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/10/world/meast/palestinian-official-dies/index.html?hpt=wo_c1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a>
<ul>
<li>The Kurdish region’s military forces, the Peshmerga Ministry, states that over 700 <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kurdish_people" title="Kurdish people">Kurds</a> have died fighting ISIL forces since June. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailystar.com.lb/News/Middle-East/2014/Dec-11/280639-over-700-iraqi-kurd-fighters-killed-since-june-isis-offensive.ashx" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Daily Star</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Russian billionaire businessman <a href="/wiki/Alisher_Usmanov" title="Alisher Usmanov">Alisher Usmanov</a> who bought the 1962 Nobel gold medal of scientist <a href="/wiki/James_Watson" title="James Watson">James Watson</a> says that he is donating it back to Watson as a gift because the "discovery of <a href="/wiki/DNA" title="DNA">DNA</a> structure must belong to him". <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-30406322" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charlene,_Princess_of_Monaco" title="Charlene, Princess of Monaco">Charlene, Princess of Monaco</a>, wife of <a href="/wiki/Albert_II,_Prince_of_Monaco" title="Albert II, Prince of Monaco">Albert II, Prince of Monaco</a>, gives birth to twins <a href="/wiki/Jacques,_Hereditary_Prince_of_Monaco" title="Jacques, Hereditary Prince of Monaco">Jacques</a> and <a href="/wiki/Princess_Gabriella,_Countess_of_Carlad%C3%A8s" title="Princess Gabriella, Countess of Carladès">Gabriella</a>. Jacques will be <a href="/wiki/Heir_apparent" title="Heir apparent">heir apparent</a> in line with male priority of <a href="/wiki/Monaco" title="Monaco">Monaco</a>'s succession laws. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/femail/article-2868690/It-s-boy-girl-Princess-Charlene-Monaco-royal-reportedly-gives-birth-twins-caesarian-section.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A wild storm hits Scotland, <a href="/wiki/Northern_England" title="Northern England">northern England</a> and <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> leaving up to 14,000 people without power in western <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-11/weather-bomb-sweeps-across-the-uk/5959594" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ebola_virus_epidemic_in_West_Africa" title="Ebola virus epidemic in West Africa">Ebola virus epidemic in West Africa</a>
<ul>
<li>Medical personnel combating the spread of the <a href="/wiki/Ebola_virus" title="Ebola virus">Ebola virus</a> are named <a href="/wiki/Time_Person_of_the_Year" title="Time Person of the Year">Time Person of the Year</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/a97aa9b320d5475ba4143d54735bce65/ebola-fighters-named-time-person-year" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Nature_(journal)" title="Nature (journal)">Nature</a></i> publishes research by the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Toronto" title="University of Toronto">University of Toronto</a> announcing the discovery of a new class of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stem_cells" title="Stem cells">stem cells</a> called F-class stem cells that have the potential to be better and safer to use in medical research. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/health/new-stem-cell-class-discovery-could-speed-up-research-1.2867063" rel="nofollow">(CBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Day" title="Human Rights Day">Human Rights Day</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> notes that torture still occurs in some countries. <a class="external text" href="http://www.amnesty.org/en/news/30-years-torture-convention-states-still-failing-obligations-2014-12-09-0" rel="nofollow">(Amnesty International)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> childrens rights activist <a href="/wiki/Malala_Yousafzai" title="Malala Yousafzai">Malala Yousafzai</a> and <a href="/wiki/Indian_people" title="Indian people">Indian</a> activist <a href="/wiki/Kailash_Satyarthi" title="Kailash Satyarthi">Kailash Satyarthi</a> receive their <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Peace_Prize" title="Nobel Peace Prize">Nobel Peace Prizes</a> in <a href="/wiki/Oslo" title="Oslo">Oslo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailytimes.com.pk/national/11-Dec-2014/malala-receives-nobel-prize" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Times Pakistan)</i></a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Poland" title="President of Poland">President of Poland</a> <a href="/wiki/Aleksander_Kwa%C5%9Bniewski" title="Aleksander Kwaśniewski">Aleksander Kwaśniewski</a> says that he authorised the <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">CIA</a> to use a "black site" in the town of <a href="/wiki/Stare_Kiejkuty_(base)" title="Stare Kiejkuty (base)">Stare Kiejkuty</a> to interrogate <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a> members in 2002. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/world/europe/la-fg-cia-torture-poland-20141210-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A court in <a href="/wiki/Langfang" title="Langfang">Langfang</a>, China, sentences former senior <a href="/wiki/Chinese_people" title="Chinese people">Chinese</a> politician <a href="/wiki/Liu_Tienan" title="Liu Tienan">Liu Tienan</a> to <a href="/wiki/Life_imprisonment" title="Life imprisonment">life imprisonment</a> after having been found guilty of corruption. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-china-30408032" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South African</a> judge rules that the prosecution can appeal the decision not to convict <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Pistorius" title="Oscar Pistorius">Oscar Pistorius</a> for the murder of <a href="/wiki/Reeva_Steenkamp" title="Reeva Steenkamp">Reeva Steenkamp</a> in 2013 to the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Appeal_of_South_Africa" title="Supreme Court of Appeal of South Africa">Supreme Court of Appeal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/world-news/pistorius-faces-murder-case-appeal-30816029.html" rel="nofollow">(Press Association via Independent)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Labor_(Israel)" title="Labor (Israel)">Labor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hatnuah" title="Hatnuah">Hatnuah</a> agree to run in a joint list for the <a href="/wiki/Israeli_legislative_election,_2015" title="Israeli legislative election, 2015">March 2015 elections in Israel</a> in a bid to establish a large center-left political bloc and remove Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> from power; <a href="/wiki/Isaac_Herzog" title="Isaac Herzog">Isaac Herzog</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tzipi_Livni" title="Tzipi Livni">Tzipi Livni</a>, should they win the elections, will share the prime ministership on rotation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesofisrael.com/herzog-livni-join-forces-to-rotate-leadership/#ixzz3Lbx8cEZq" rel="nofollow">(The Times of Israel)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mauritian_general_election,_2014" title="Mauritian general election, 2014">Mauritian general election</a>
<ul>
<li>The opposition <a href="/wiki/Militant_Socialist_Movement" title="Militant Socialist Movement">MMM</a>-<a href="/wiki/Parti_Mauricien_Social_D%C3%A9mocrate" title="Parti Mauricien Social Démocrate">PMSD</a> coalition wins a majority in the <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Mauritius)" title="National Assembly (Mauritius)">National Assembly</a>, ending the ruling <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(Mauritius)" title="Labour Party (Mauritius)">MLP</a>-<a href="/wiki/Mauritian_Militant_Movement" title="Mauritian Militant Movement">MMM</a> alliance's plan to grant more powers to the office of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Mauritius" title="President of Mauritius">President</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/idUSKBN0JP0PU20141211?irpc=932" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 11, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-11</span>)</span> (Thursday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_11&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_11&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_11&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban_insurgency" title="Taliban insurgency">Taliban insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomber" title="Suicide bomber">suicide bomber</a> kills at least six <a href="/wiki/Afghan_National_Army" title="Afghan National Army">Afghan National Army</a> soldiers in Tangi Tarakhil on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Kabul" title="Kabul">Kabul</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20141211-taliban-suicide-blast-kills-six-afghan-soldiers-kabul/?aef_campaign_date=2014-12-11&amp;aef_campaign_ref=partage_aef&amp;ns_campaign=reseaux_sociaux&amp;ns_linkname=editorial&amp;ns_mchannel=social&amp;ns_source=twitter#?aef_campaign_date=2014-12-11&amp;aef_campaign_ref=partage_aef&amp;ns_campaign=reseaux_sociaux&amp;ns_linkname=editorial&amp;ns_mchannel=social&amp;ns_source=twitter&amp;_suid=141827533791008981681490221784" rel="nofollow">(AFP via France 24)</a></li>
<li>A suicide bomber attacks a cultural center putting on a play critical of terrorist attacks, killing a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_people" title="German people">German</a> national and wounding 16 others. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-12/afghanistan-suicide-bomber-kabul-france-condemns/5962130" rel="nofollow">(Reuters/AFP via ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Obama_Administration" title="Obama Administration">Obama Administration</a> orders the closing of the last US-run detention facility in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Bagram_Airfield" title="Bagram Airfield">Bagram Airfield</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nydailynews.com/news/world/u-s-closes-afghan-bagram-prison-no-detainees-held-article-1.2042422" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Daily News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist_insurgency_in_Nigeria" title="Islamist insurgency in Nigeria">Islamist insurgency in Nigeria</a>:
<ul>
<li>Two bombs explode in the central <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigerian</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Jos" title="Jos">Jos</a> with at least 40 people dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/reuters/article-2870549/Blasts-kill-32-Nigerian-city-Jos.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A study by <a href="/wiki/BBC_World_Service" title="BBC World Service">BBC World Service</a> and <a href="/wiki/King%27s_College_London" title="King's College London">King's College London</a> finds the death toll from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jihadist" title="Jihadist">jihadist</a> attacks during the month of November surpassed 5,000. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-30080914" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The oldest <a href="/wiki/Time_capsule" title="Time capsule">time capsule</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> is unearthed at the <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts_State_House" title="Massachusetts State House">Massachusetts State House</a>. The capsule was first buried in the <a href="/wiki/Cornerstone" title="Cornerstone">cornerstone</a> by <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Adams" title="Samuel Adams">Samuel Adams</a> in 1795 and reburied by <a href="/wiki/Henry_Gardner" title="Henry Gardner">Henry Gardner</a> in 1855. Wrapped in cowhide, four silver coins fell out when it was found. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/US/oldest-time-capsule-us-unearthed-massachusetts-state-house/story?id=27539479" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/11/us/boston-time-capsule-paul-revere-sam-adams/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">American</a> state of <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> prepares for its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/December_2014_West_Coast_storm" title="December 2014 West Coast storm">worst storm in five years</a> with schools closed in the <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Bay_Area" title="San Francisco Bay Area">San Francisco Bay Area</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/weather/2014/12/10/california-storm/20187287/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hagupit_(2014)" title="Typhoon Hagupit (2014)">Typhoon Hagupit (Ruby)</a>
<ul>
<li>The death toll from Typhoon Hagupit rises to 18. <a class="external text" href="http://www.philstar.com/headlines/2014/12/11/1401486/ruby-death-toll-climbs-18" rel="nofollow">(Phil Star)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Truth_Commission" title="National Truth Commission">National Truth Commission</a> set up to investigate human rights abuses by the <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_military_government" title="Brazilian military government">Brazilian military government</a> of 1964-1985 draws a link between regime era killings and kidnappings to the high number of killings by <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Brazil" title="Law enforcement in Brazil">today's police force</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/the_americas/report-on-brazil-dictatorship-urges-police-reform/2014/12/11/61607cb8-8147-11e4-b936-f3afab0155a7_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/British_people" title="British people">British</a> radio DJ <a href="/wiki/Ray_Teret" title="Ray Teret">Ray Teret</a> is jailed for 25 years for a series of sexual assaults on 11 girls in the 1960s and 1970s conducted in association with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jimmy_Saville" title="Jimmy Saville">Jimmy Saville</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.billboard.com/biz/articles/news/legal-and-management/6405570/radio-dj-ray-teret-friend-of-jimmy-savile-jailed-for" rel="nofollow">(Billboard)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Law enforcement in the United Kingdom">British police</a> charge Aravindan Balakrishnan or <i>Comrade Bala</i> with 25 offences including rape in relation to the <a href="/wiki/Lambeth_slavery_case" title="Lambeth slavery case">Lambeth slavery case</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ctvnews.ca/world/comrade-bala-charged-with-rape-cruelty-in-u-k-enslavement-case-1.2143159" rel="nofollow">(AP via CTV News)</a></li>
<li>Alleged <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> serial killer, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Sailson_Jose_das_Gracas&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Sailson Jose das Gracas (page does not exist)">Sailson Jose das Gracas</a>, confesses to 42 murders in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/11/us-brazil-serialkiller-idUSKBN0JP23B20141211" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>In <i>R. v. Fearon</i>, the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Canada" title="Supreme Court of Canada">Supreme Court of Canada</a> rules by 4–3 vote that searching for cell phones without a warrant during an arrest does not violate the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Section_Eight_of_the_Canadian_Charter_of_Rights_and_Freedoms" title="Section Eight of the Canadian Charter of Rights and Freedoms">Section Eight of the Canadian Charter of Rights and Freedoms</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://globalnews.ca/news/1721307/what-rules-must-police-follow-to-search-a-cellphone-during-arrest/" rel="nofollow">(Global News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Hong_Kong_protests" title="2014 Hong Kong protests">2014 Hong Kong protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Authorities start clearing the main protest site in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> following a recent court order for protesters to vacate the site in <a href="/wiki/Admiralty,_Hong_Kong" title="Admiralty, Hong Kong">Admiralty</a> area. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsj.com/articles/clearance-of-main-hong-kong-protest-site-begins-1418265523?mod=ask" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> narrowly passes a budget spending bill to avoid a potential <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_government" title="United States government">government</a> shutdown. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/first-read/deadline-looming-government-funding-bill-passes-house-n266386" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_Navy" title="US Navy">US Navy</a> initiates the operation of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Laser_weapon" title="Laser weapon">laser weapons</a>. The first use is to protect ships deployed in the <a href="/wiki/Persian_Gulf" title="Persian Gulf">Persian Gulf</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/tech/2014/12/11/navy-declares-laser-weapons-ready-to-protect-ships-in-persian-gulf/?intcmp=features" rel="nofollow">(Military.com via FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment">Sony Pictures Entertainment</a> reportedly shuts production on several sets because of computer network issues regarding employee disbursement of pay following a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">massive computer hack</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/entertainment/2014/12/12/hacked-sony-reportedly-shuts-production/" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Thousands of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_people" title="Italian people">Italians</a> take to the streets in 50 cities as part of a <a href="/wiki/General_strike" title="General strike">general strike</a> protesting new labour laws. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-13/thousands-protest-against-italian-government/5965086" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>Wall Street sees its worst week in three years as oil prices continue to collapse. The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> sheds 315 points, or 1.8%, to 17280. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxbusiness.com/markets/2014/12/12/us-stock-index-futures-lower-as-oil-continues-rout/?intcmp=bigtopmarketfeatures&amp;intcmp=bigtopteaserside" rel="nofollow">(FOX Business)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Lake_Tanganyika#Transport" title="Lake Tanganyika">ferry MV Mutambala capsizes</a> on <a href="/wiki/Lake_Tanganyika" title="Lake Tanganyika">Lake Tanganyika</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> leaving at least 26 dead. <a class="external text" href="http://radiookapi.net/actualite/2014/12/12/naufrage-du-bateau-mv-mutambala-sur-le-lac-tanganyika-26-morts/" rel="nofollow">(Radiookapi.net)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An unknown person shoots four people outside of Rosemary Anderson High School, an alternative high school in <a href="/wiki/Portland,_Oregon" title="Portland, Oregon">Portland, Oregon</a>. Police later question a 22-year-old man. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/12/us/portland-school-shooting/index.html?hpt=hp_t1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.msn.com/en-us/news/crime/two-shot-outside-portland-oregon-high-school-police/ar-BBgI6Vo" rel="nofollow">(MSN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/6ffe77f0d02f4c618e9608c0788fb822/police-say-oregon-shooting-appears-gang-related" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>Prosecutors at Sary-Arqa District Court in <a href="/wiki/Astana" title="Astana">Astana</a> charge 30-year-old Yevgeny Vdovenko, a Kazakh citizen, of intentional and illegal participation in a military conflict abroad because he had fought alongside pro-Russian separatists in eastern <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/kazakh-fighter-ukraine-trial/26739397.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> man throws a chemical substance believed to be acid at an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli" title="Israeli">Israeli</a> family that stopped to pick up a hitchhiker. No terrorist groups claim credit for the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/12/us-mideast-palestinians-israel-idUSKBN0JQ19E20141212" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Torrent site <a href="/wiki/IsoHunt" title="IsoHunt">isoHunt</a> appears to have unofficially resurrected <a href="/wiki/The_Pirate_Bay" title="The Pirate Bay">The Pirate Bay</a> at a site which turns out serving new content. <a class="external text" href="http://venturebeat.com/2014/12/12/isohunt-unofficially-resurrects-the-pirate-bay/" rel="nofollow">(VB News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> announces its upcoming <a href="/wiki/Windows_10" title="Windows 10">Windows 10</a> consumer version preview for January 21. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/tech/2014/12/12/microsoft-to-spill-windows-10-beans-jan-21" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
