<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_13&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban_insurgency" title="Taliban insurgency">Taliban insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>Gunmen assassinate Atiqullah Rawoofi, the head of the Secretariat of the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Afghanistan" title="Supreme Court of Afghanistan">Supreme Court of Afghanistan</a>, in the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Kabul" title="Kabul">Kabul</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/A/AS_AFGHANISTAN?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>Twenty-one people die in attacks across <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> including two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Army" title="U.S. Army">American soldiers</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/at-least-21-die-in-attacks-in-kabul-other-parts-of-afghanistan/2014/12/13/927ee56a-a3b6-4ed4-9075-c6f71b381457_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_State_in_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State in Iraq and the Levant</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> officials claim that ISIL have shot down a military helicopter near <a href="/wiki/Samarra" title="Samarra">Samarra</a>, killing both pilots. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted2.ap.org/APDEFAULT/3d281c11a96b4ad082fe88aa0db04305/Article_2014-12-13-ML--Islamic%20State/id-7ebe7cd6a85c4b6fa276937ef5c5f67b" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>'s most successful television show, <i><a href="/wiki/Wetten,_dass..%3F" title="Wetten, dass..?">Wetten, dass..?</a></i>, ends after a 33-year-run. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/E/EU_GERMANY_STUNT_SHOW?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">Landslides</a> caused by heavy rain in <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Indonesia_landslides" title="2014 Indonesia landslides">kill</a> at least 17 people with a hundred still unaccounted for. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/A/AS_INDONESIA_LANDSLIDE?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/asiapacific/8-dead-100-missing-in/1527318.html?cid=TWTCNA&amp;utm_source=dlvr.it&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Channel News Asia)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30459175" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Philippines_v._China" title="Philippines v. China">Philippines v. China</a></i>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> files an intervention in the arbitration case about the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a> with Vietnam rejecting <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>'s claims. <a class="external text" href="http://mobile.bloomberg.com/news/2014-12-12/south-china-sea-tensions-flare-as-vietnam-files-stance-to-court.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/India%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="India–Russia relations">India and Russia</a> sign deals on infrastructure, nuclear energy, and defence. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/11/us-india-russia-idUSKBN0JO2C620141211?feedType=RSS" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The wife of <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>'s crown prince <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maha_Vajiralongkorn" title="Maha Vajiralongkorn">Maha Vajiralongkorn</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Princess_Srirasmi" title="Princess Srirasmi">Princess Srirasmi</a>, resigns her royal status following a corruption probe of her relatives. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_of_Thailand" title="King of Thailand">King of Thailand</a> <a href="/wiki/Bhumibol_Adulyadej" title="Bhumibol Adulyadej">Bhumibol Adulyadej</a> grants her a divorce. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-13/thailand-crown-princes-wife-resigns-her-royal-title/5965214" rel="nofollow">(AFP via ABC News Australia)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/2014/12/13/thailands-crown-prince-divorces-wife" rel="nofollow">(AAP via SBS)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Geminids" title="Geminids">Geminids</a> <a href="/wiki/Meteor_shower" title="Meteor shower">meteor shower</a> reaches its peak this weekend. <a class="external text" href="http://boingboing.net/2014/12/12/geminid-meteor-showers-peak-th.html?utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+boingboing%2FiBag+%28Boing+Boing%29" rel="nofollow">(Boing Boing)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Mariota" title="Marcus Mariota">Marcus Mariota</a> of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Oregon" title="University of Oregon">University of Oregon</a> <a href="/wiki/Oregon_Ducks_football" title="Oregon Ducks football">football team</a> wins the 2014 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heisman_trophy" title="Heisman trophy">Heisman trophy</a> for the best player in <a href="/wiki/College_football" title="College football">college football</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/sports/2014/12/13/oregon-qb-marcus-mariota-wins-heisman-trophy/" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 14, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-14</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_14&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_14&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_14&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>

</td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>:
<ul>
<li>A battle between <a href="/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad" title="Bashar al-Assad">Bashar al-Assad</a> loyalist forces and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist" title="Islamist">Islamist</a> rebels in <a href="/wiki/Aleppo_Governorate" title="Aleppo Governorate">Aleppo Governorate</a> leave 34 rebels dead and 3 loyalist fighters captured. <a class="external text" href="http://latino.foxnews.com/latino/news/2014/12/14/34-islamist-rebels-die-in-combat-with-syrian-army-in-aleppo/" rel="nofollow">(EFE via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Miss_World_2014" title="Miss World 2014">Miss World 2014</a> crowns <a href="/wiki/Rolene_Strauss" title="Rolene Strauss">Rolene Strauss</a>, <a href="/wiki/Miss_South_Africa" title="Miss South Africa">Miss South Africa</a>, in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2014/12/14/world/feat-miss-world-2014/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Archaeologists reconstruct two giant statues of <a href="/wiki/Amenhotep_III" title="Amenhotep III">Amenhotep III</a>, toppled by an earthquake at the Nile River in 1200 BC. The team's restoration project re-erected surviving fragments at the northern gate of the king's funerary temple. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-2873578/Colossal-statue-Amenhotep-III-unveiled-Egypt.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Daily Mail)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>European private equity firm <a href="/wiki/BC_Partners" title="BC Partners">BC Partners</a> agrees to buy American pet supplies retail chain <a href="/wiki/PetSmart" title="PetSmart">PetSmart</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_dollars" title="United States dollars">$</a>8.7 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.nytimes.com/2014/12/14/petsmart-to-sell-itself-to-investor-group-for-8-7-billion/?partner=rss&amp;emc=rss&amp;_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Eleven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Egyptian_people" title="Egyptian people">Egyptian</a> fishermen drown after their boat sinks in the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Suez" title="Gulf of Suez">Gulf of Suez</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/350d6a68f1744564a441569732edb208/officials-11-egypt-fishermen-drown-boat-sinks" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>The death toll from a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Indonesia_landslides" title="2014 Indonesia landslides">landslide</a> in central <a href="/wiki/Java" title="Java">Java</a> in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> rises to 24 with scores still missing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/scores-missing-indonesia-landslide-death-toll-hits-24-n267681" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via NBC News)</a></li>
<li>The death toll of a <a href="/wiki/Lake_Tanganyika#Transport" title="Lake Tanganyika">capsized ferry MV Mutambala</a> on December 12 in <a href="/wiki/Lake_Tanganyika" title="Lake Tanganyika">Lake Tanganyika</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> rises to 129 with authorities continuing to search for bodies or survivors. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-30470079" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Environment</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Angalifu" title="Angalifu">Angalifu</a>, a male of the <a href="/wiki/Critically_endangered" title="Critically endangered">critically endangered</a> <a href="/wiki/Northern_white_rhinoceros" title="Northern white rhinoceros">northern white rhinoceros</a>, dies at the <a href="/wiki/San_Diego_Zoo_Safari_Park" title="San Diego Zoo Safari Park">San Diego Zoo Safari Park</a>. The remaining rhinoceroses are one female at the Zoo (<a href="/wiki/Nola_(rhinoceros)" title="Nola (rhinoceros)">Nola</a>), three at a zoo in the Czech Republic, and one male at a Kenyan preserve (<a href="/wiki/Sudan_(rhinoceros)" title="Sudan (rhinoceros)">Sudan</a>). <a class="external text" href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2014/12/15/northern-white-rhino-dies_n_6328156.html" rel="nofollow">(Huffington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/2014_United_Nations_Climate_Change_Conference" title="2014 United Nations Climate Change Conference">adopts</a> a format for national pledges to tackle climate change after meetings extend into the weekend at the conference held in <a href="/wiki/Lima" title="Lima">Lima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/science-environment-30468048?ns_mchannel=social&amp;ns_campaign=bbc_breaking&amp;ns_source=twitter&amp;ns_linkname=news_central" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> police arrest 24 journalists, all of whom are supporters of <a href="/wiki/Fethullah_G%C3%BClen" title="Fethullah Gülen">Fethullah Gülen</a> who is a rival of current <a href="/wiki/President_of_Turkey" title="President of Turkey">Turkish President</a> <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a> and is currently in self-imposed exile in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/reu-turkish-police-raid-media-close-to-cleric-rival-gulen-detain-twenty-three/2558278.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japanese_general_election,_2014" title="Japanese general election, 2014">Japanese general election, 2014</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japanese_people" title="Japanese people">Japanese</a> citizens vote in a general election. <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shinzo_Abe" title="Shinzo Abe">Shinzo Abe</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan)">Liberal Democratic Party</a> and its <a href="/wiki/Komeito" title="Komeito">junior coalition partner</a> win 325 seats out of 475 and thus a new term. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30444230" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Laurent_Lamothe" title="Laurent Lamothe">Laurent Lamothe</a> resigns as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Haiti" title="Prime Minister of Haiti">Prime Minister of Haiti</a> along with several ministers following violent protests and a commission's call for him to step down. The protesters have been demanding the holding of early elections. <a class="external text" href="http://townhall.com/news/politics-elections/2014/12/14/haiti-awaits-pm-speech-amid-political-discontent-n1931598" rel="nofollow">(<i>TownHall</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">NBA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kobe_Bryant" title="Kobe Bryant">Kobe Bryant</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Lakers" title="Los Angeles Lakers">Los Angeles Lakers</a> moves to third on the all-time <a href="/wiki/Point_(basketball)" title="Point (basketball)">point scorer</a> list overtaking <a href="/wiki/Michael_Jordan" title="Michael Jordan">Michael Jordan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sportsfan.com.au/bryant-passes-jordan-on-all-time-nba-list/tabid/91/newsid/150148/default.aspx?utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=feed&amp;utm_campaign=Feed%3A+BigpondsportcomLatestNews+%28BigPondSport.com+Latest+News%29" rel="nofollow">(AFP via SportsFan)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_15&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A fire at a <a href="/wiki/Karaoke" title="Karaoke">karaoke</a> bar in <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Henan" title="Henan">Henan</a> province kills at least 11 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehindu.com/news/international/11-dead-in-china-karaoke-bar-fire/article6692691.ece" rel="nofollow">(IANS via <i>The Hindu</i>)</a></li>
<li>An emergency rescue <a href="/wiki/SMURD" title="SMURD">SMURD</a> helicopter crashes into <a href="/wiki/Lake_Siutghiol" title="Lake Siutghiol">Lake Siutghiol</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Constan%C5%A3a_County" title="Constanţa County">Constanţa County</a>, <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a> with four people killed. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/helicopter-crashes-lake-romania-missing-27612089" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a></li>
<li>The death toll of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Indonesia_landslide" title="2014 Indonesia landslide">2014 Indonesia landslide</a> rises to 56. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2014/12/15/death-toll-from-indonesian-mudslide-rises-to-51-as-rain-halts-search-for-dozens/?intcmp=latestnews" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippine</a> prosecutors charge a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Marine" title="United States Marine">United States Marine</a> with murder over the <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Jennifer_Laude" title="Death of Jennifer Laude">death of Jennifer Laude</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Filipino_people" title="Filipino people">Filipino</a> <a href="/wiki/Transgender" title="Transgender">transgender</a> woman. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/us-marine-charged-with-murder-of-filipino-transgender/2014/12/15/ddef5b7c-8427-11e4-abcf-5a3d7b3b20b8_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Authorized by the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Convention_on_the_Law_of_the_Sea" title="United Nations Convention on the Law of the Sea">United Nations Convention on the Law of the Sea</a>, Denmark becomes the first country to <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_the_Arctic" title="Territorial claims in the Arctic">officially submit a claim</a> on the <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">North Pole</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2014/12/15/Denmark-files-first-official-claim-on-North-Pole/7551418671808/?r=83761289833346" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li>About ten thousand people, including those of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Patriotic_Europeans_Against_the_Islamization_of_the_Occident" title="Patriotic Europeans Against the Islamization of the Occident">Patriotic Europeans Against the Islamization of the Occident</a> (PEGIDA), protest in Germany against the presence of Muslims. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thetelegram.com/News/Canada---World/2014-12-15/article-3977468/Anti-Islam-protests-grow-in-Germany/1" rel="nofollow">(The Telegram)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Sydney_hostage_crisis" title="2014 Sydney hostage crisis">2014 Sydney hostage crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>A gunman, <a href="/wiki/Man_Haron_Monis" title="Man Haron Monis">Man Haron Monis</a>, takes 17 people hostage at <a href="/wiki/Lindt_%26_Spr%C3%BCngli" title="Lindt &amp; Sprüngli">Lindt Chocolate Café</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Martin_Place,_Sydney" title="Martin Place, Sydney">Martin Place</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://m.bbc.com/news/world-australia-30473983" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-15/sydney-siege-hostages-cafe-martin-place-police-operation/5967232" rel="nofollow">(ABC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldsun.com.au/news/national/sydney-siege-what-we-know-what-we-dont/story-fni0xqrb-1227156965180" rel="nofollow">(<i>Melbourne Herald-Sun</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Montgomery_County,_Pennsylvania_shootings" title="Montgomery County, Pennsylvania shootings">Montgomery County, Pennsylvania shootings</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Spree_killer" title="Spree killer">shooting spree</a> kills six people throughout <a href="/wiki/Montgomery_County,_Pennsylvania" title="Montgomery County, Pennsylvania">Montgomery County</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</a> suburbs. The suspect, Bradley William Stone, remains <a href="/wiki/Fugitive#Terminology" title="Fugitive">at large</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://6abc.com/news/montco-shootings-4th-scene-in-pennsburg;-suspect-barricade-in-souderton/436923/" rel="nofollow">(WPVI-TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.philly.com/philly/news/20141216_Manhunt_continues_after_6_die_in_shooting_spree.html" rel="nofollow">(Philadelphia Inquirer)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">Supreme Court of the United States</a> rules by an <a href="/wiki/Heien_v._North_Carolina" title="Heien v. North Carolina">8–1 vote</a> that <a href="/wiki/Evidence_(law)" title="Evidence (law)">evidence</a> collected based on a reasonable misinterpretation of the law can be used at trial and is not deemed an <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Amendment_to_the_United_States_Constitution" title="Fourth Amendment to the United States Constitution">unreasonable search or seizure</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsj.com/articles/supreme-court-gives-police-more-leeway-in-traffic-stop-case-1418665366?mod=wsj_hppmiddlenexttowhatsnewssecond" rel="nofollow">(Wall Street Journal)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/news/volokh-conspiracy/wp/2014/12/15/reasonable-mistake-of-law-can-generate-reasonable-suspicion-supreme-court-holds/" rel="nofollow">(Washington Post)</a></li>
<li>An appellate court in Vietnam upholds a 30-year prison sentence and convictions for <a href="/wiki/Nguyen_Duc_Kien" title="Nguyen Duc Kien">Nguyen Duc Kien</a>, a former businessman. <a class="external text" href="http://tuoitrenews.vn/society/24719/vietnam-court-upholds-exbanking-tycoons-30year-jail-term" rel="nofollow">(Tuoi Tre)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Hong_Kong_protests" title="2014 Hong Kong protests">2014 Hong Kong protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Authorities remove the last remaining protest camp, the one at <a href="/wiki/Causeway_Bay" title="Causeway Bay">Causeway Bay</a>, Hong Kong. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsj.com/articles/hong-kong-police-clear-last-protest-site-1418616478?tesla=y" rel="nofollow">(Wall Street Journal)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30474687" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> approves <a href="/wiki/Vivek_Murthy" title="Vivek Murthy">Vivek Murthy</a>'s nomination as <a href="/wiki/Surgeon_General_of_the_United_States" title="Surgeon General of the United States">Surgeon General</a> by a 51–43 vote. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/surgeon-general-nominee-finally-has-confirmation-vote/" rel="nofollow">(CBS)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Peshawar_school_attack" title="2014 Peshawar school attack">2014 Peshawar school attack</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> gunmen storm one of the military-run <a href="/wiki/Army_Public_Schools_%26_Colleges_System" title="Army Public Schools &amp; Colleges System">Army Public Schools</a> in the Pakistani city of <a href="/wiki/Peshawar" title="Peshawar">Peshawar</a>, killing at least 141, including 132 children and nine employees, with most of five hundred students evacuated. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-pakistan-school-idUSKBN0JU0JO20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30491435" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/12/17/world/asia/taliban-attack-pakistani-school.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow"><i>(The New York Times)</i></a></li>
<li>The shooting ends with all six gunmen dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.co.uk/peshawar-school-attack-pakistan-authorities-claim-victory-after-killing-all-six-taliban-militants-1479785" rel="nofollow">(International Business Times)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>Around one hundred Syrian soldiers and eighty Islamist fighters die in a <a href="/wiki/Second_Siege_of_Wadi_Deif" title="Second Siege of Wadi Deif">two-day battle for Wadi Deif</a>, with the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_Front_(Syria)" title="Islamic Front (Syria)">Islamic Front</a> capturing over 120 government soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-mideast-crisis-base-idUSKBN0JU0WV20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Terrorism_in_Yemen" title="Terrorism in Yemen">Terrorism in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>A pair of car bombs kill 20 children and 11 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Houthi_rebellion" title="Houthi rebellion">Houthi militants</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Radaa" title="Radaa">Radaa</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Bayda%27_Governorate" title="Al Bayda' Governorate">central Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/16/world/meast/yemen-violence/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gaza%E2%80%93Israel_conflict" title="Gaza–Israel conflict">Gaza–Israel conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>Israeli military troops kill one Palestinian man in a <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a> refugee camp. Israeli sources claim the man threw an explosive device at an army patrol. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-mideast-palestinians-israel-idUSKBN0JU0FR20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Russian_financial_crisis" title="2014 Russian financial crisis">2014 Russian financial crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bank_of_Russia" title="Bank of Russia">Bank of Russia</a> announces an increase of its key interest rate, the <a href="/wiki/Moscow_Exchange#Foreign_Exchange_and_Money_market" title="Moscow Exchange">Russian weekly</a> <a href="/wiki/Repurchase_agreement" title="Repurchase agreement">repo rate</a>, from 10.5 to 17 percent as an emergency move to halt the collapse of the <a href="/wiki/Russian_ruble" title="Russian ruble">ruble</a>'s value and, thereby, stabilize the Russian economy. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/business/international/russia-hikes-key-rate-to/1531324.html" rel="nofollow">(Channel News Asia)</a></li>
<li>Despite rate hike, the ruble falls to <span class="error" style="font-size:inherit">{{currency}} – invalid amount (<a href="/wiki/Template:Currency/doc#Error_messages" title="Template:Currency/doc">help</a>)</span> per US dollar and <span class="error" style="font-size:inherit">{{currency}} – invalid amount (<a href="/wiki/Template:Currency/doc#Error_messages" title="Template:Currency/doc">help</a>)</span> per Euro. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-russia-rouble-exchange-idUSKBN0JU0KO20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Music_Entertainment" title="Sony Music Entertainment">Sony Music Entertainment</a> gives Chinese online company <a href="/wiki/Tencent" title="Tencent">Tencent</a> rights to distribute its music catalogue. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/tencent-sony-music-idUSL3N0U02WT20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The price of <a href="/wiki/Brent_Crude" title="Brent Crude">Brent Crude</a> oil drops to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_dollars" title="United States dollars">$</a>55–60 per barrel for the first time since 2009. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-markets-oil-idUSKBN0JU0BO20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The court jury finds <a href="/wiki/Apple_Inc." title="Apple Inc.">Apple Inc.</a> in a nine-year lawsuit not guilty of violating antitrust laws and deleting music content for security reasons. <a class="external text" href="http://arstechnica.com/tech-policy/2014/12/jury-finds-for-apple-in-itunes-case-throws-out-billion-dollar-lawsuit/" rel="nofollow">(Ars Technica)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.businessweek.com/news/2014-12-16/apple-prevails-at-1-billion-trial-over-digital-music" rel="nofollow">(BusinessWeek)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.nydailynews.com/news/national/apple-wins-digital-music-u-s-antitrust-trial-article-1.2047274" rel="nofollow">(NY Daily News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/American_Apparel" title="American Apparel">American Apparel</a> fires its founder <a href="/wiki/Dov_Charney" title="Dov Charney">Dov Charney</a> as its Chief Executive Officer after months of suspension. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-american-apparel-managementchanges-idUSKBN0JU2J220141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A tunnel collapse traps twelve <a href="/wiki/Vietnamese_people" title="Vietnamese people">Vietnamese</a> workers, including one woman, at a construction site of a hydropower plant located in the <a href="/wiki/Central_Highlands_(Vietnam)" title="Central Highlands (Vietnam)">Central Highlands</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thanhniennews.com/society/12-workers-trapped-after-tunnel-collapse-in-vietnam-hydropower-project-35366.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Thanh Nien</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Sydney_hostage_crisis" title="2014 Sydney hostage crisis">2014 Sydney hostage crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The hostage situation ends with gunman <a href="/wiki/Man_Haron_Monis" title="Man Haron Monis">Man Haron Monis</a> and two hostages dead and four others injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/15/world/asia/australia-sydney-hostage-situation/index.html?hpt=hp_t1" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2014-12-15/sydney-siege-hostages-cafe-martin-place-police-operation/5967232" rel="nofollow">(ABC Australia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel_Police" title="Israel Police">Israel Police</a> arrest ten members of <a href="/wiki/Lehava" title="Lehava">Lehava</a>, a right-wing organisation that opposes integration of Arabs and Jews, for last month's arson on an Arab–Jewish school. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesofisrael.com/police-arrest-head-of-anti-assimilation-group-lehava/" rel="nofollow">(Times of Israel)</a></li>
<li>India declares a ban on <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> after an engineer was detained for campaigning on behalf of the group on Twitter. Officials worry that such ban will endanger thirty-nine men, believed to be held hostage by the group. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-mideast-crisis-india-idUSKBN0JU0TV20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Montgomery_County,_Pennsylvania_shootings" title="Montgomery County, Pennsylvania shootings">Montgomery County, Pennsylvania shootings</a>
<ul>
<li>The Montgomery County District Attorney reports that Bradley Stone, suspected in the killing of his ex-wife and five of her family members Monday, has been found dead in the woods near his home in <a href="/wiki/Pennsburg,_Pennsylvania" title="Pennsburg, Pennsylvania">Pennsburg, Pa.</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcphiladelphia.com/news/local/Montgomery-County-Shooting-Spree-Suspect-Bradley-Stone-Found-Dead-in-Woods-285983841.html#ixzz3M5hZfi4U" rel="nofollow">(NBC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://venturebeat.com/2014/12/18/nasa-has-emailed-a-wrench-to-astronauts-in-space/" rel="nofollow">(Venturebeat)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Same-sex marriage in the United Kingdom">Same-sex marriage</a> becomes legal in <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Marriage_and_Civil_Partnership_(Scotland)_Act_2014" title="Marriage and Civil Partnership (Scotland) Act 2014">Marriage and Civil Partnership (Scotland) Act 2014</a> coming into effect. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/uk-scotland-scotland-politics-30486804" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Judge <a href="/wiki/Arthur_J._Schwab" title="Arthur J. Schwab">Arthur J. Schwab</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_Western_District_of_Pennsylvania" title="United States District Court for the Western District of Pennsylvania">US District Court of Pennsylvania</a> declares President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>'s executive order on immigration <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unconstitutional" title="Unconstitutional">unconstitutional</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/us-usa-courts-immigration-idUSKBN0JU2GX20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>For the first time, <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> emailed <a href="/wiki/Household_hardware" title="Household hardware">hardware</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Wrench" title="Wrench">wrench</a>, to the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> that was fabricated on the ISS's <a href="/wiki/Weightlessness" title="Weightlessness">Zero Gravity</a> <a href="/wiki/3D_printing" title="3D printing">3D printer</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://3dprint.com/32269/made-in-space-emails-wrench/" rel="nofollow">(3dPrint.com)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://medium.com/backchannel/how-we-email-hardware-to-space-7d46eed00c98" rel="nofollow">(Medium.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Peshawar_school_attack" title="2014 Peshawar school attack">2014 Peshawar school attack</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> lifts the <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Pakistan" title="Capital punishment in Pakistan">moratorium</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment" title="Capital punishment">death penalty</a> for terror-related cases following the <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban's</a> assault on a school in <a href="/wiki/Peshawar" title="Peshawar">Peshawar</a> on Tuesday that killed 141, including 132 children. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2014/dec/17/pakistan-school-massacre-taliban-nawaz-sharif-lift-death-penalty-ban" rel="nofollow">(The Guardian)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li>Sony cancels the <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> sneak preview of the upcoming 2014 film <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Interview_(2014_film)" title="The Interview (2014 film)">The Interview</a></i>, originally scheduled for December 18, due to threatening messages by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(computer_security)" title="Hacker (computer security)">hackers</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/life/movies/2014/12/16/sony-hackers-threaten-movie-theaters/20485591/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
<li>Sony cancels the release of <i>The Interview</i>, originally scheduled for <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a> 2014. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2014/12/17/media/the-interview-sony-theater-owners/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Spanish energy company <a href="/wiki/Repsol" title="Repsol">Repsol</a> acquires Canadian energy producer <a href="/wiki/Talisman_Energy" title="Talisman Energy">Talisman Energy</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_dollars" title="United States dollars">$</a>13 billion including debt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/16/talisman-ma-repsol-idUSL6N0TZ2QF20141216" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> re-establish <a href="/wiki/Cuba%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Cuba–United States relations">diplomatic relations</a> after severing them 55 years ago. An <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Havana" title="Embassy of the United States, Havana">American embassy</a> will open in <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">Havana</a> and talks to lift the <a href="/wiki/United_States_embargo_against_Cuba" title="United States embargo against Cuba">embargo</a> will begin. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/cheats/2014/12/17/alan-gross-released-from-cuban-prison.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Beast</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> removes <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> from its list of terrorist organizations. <a class="external text" href="http://rt.com/news/215143-hamas-off-terror-list/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Reuters</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="Communist Party of China">Chinese Communist Party</a>, through the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_People%27s_Procuratorate" title="Supreme People's Procuratorate">Supreme People's Procuratorate</a>, indicts former <a href="/wiki/Nanjing" title="Nanjing">Nanjing</a> mayor <a href="/wiki/Ji_Jianye" title="Ji Jianye">Ji Jianye</a> on bribery and corruption. <a class="external text" href="http://www.denverpost.com/nationworld/ci_27152947/china-indicts-former-mayor-nanjing-corruption-charges" rel="nofollow">(AP via Denver Post)</a></li>
<li>The U.S. attorney's office indicts Gregory Conigliaro and Barry Cadden, co-founders of the <a href="/wiki/New_England_Compounding_Center" title="New England Compounding Center">New England Compounding Center</a> in <a href="/wiki/Framingham,_Massachusetts" title="Framingham, Massachusetts">Framingham, Mass.</a>, along with 12 former employees, on federal racketeering for a <a href="/wiki/Meningitis" title="Meningitis">fungal meningitis</a> <a href="/wiki/New_England_Compounding_Center_meningitis_outbreak" title="New England Compounding Center meningitis outbreak">outbreak</a> that killed 64 people in seven states in the fall of 2012. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/b1605686213745359eafdaad2964f361/pharmacy-owners-arrested-12-meningitis-outbreak" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Hellenic_Parliament" title="Hellenic Parliament">Parliament of Greece</a> fails <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greek_presidential_election,_2014" title="Greek presidential election, 2014">to elect a new president</a> in the first round of voting. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/greek-lawmakers-vote-crucial-presidency-ballot-27655961" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>'s independent ethics investigator <a href="/wiki/Michael_J._Garcia" title="Michael J. Garcia">Michael J. Garcia</a> resigns from that position in protest over the organization's handling of <a href="/wiki/Garcia_Report" title="Garcia Report">his compiled report on corruption allegations</a> in connection with the bidding process for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018</a> and <a href="/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2022 FIFA World Cup">2022</a> <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cups</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/sport/0/football/30522170" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gumsuri_kidnapping" title="Gumsuri kidnapping">Gumsuri kidnapping</a>
<ul>
<li>News emerges, after survivors reach the city of <a href="/wiki/Maiduguri" title="Maiduguri">Maiduguri</a>, that suspected <a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a> militants stormed the remote village of Gumsuri in north-eastern <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> on December 14, killing at least 33 people and kidnapping about 200. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-30529178" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The price of <a href="/wiki/Brent_Crude" title="Brent Crude">Brent Crude</a> oil rises to <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">$</a>61+ per barrel as companies cut upstream investments. <a class="external text" href="http://ca.reuters.com/article/businessNews/idCAKBN0JW0BC20141218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>US clothing company <a href="/wiki/Gap_Inc." title="Gap Inc.">Gap Inc.</a> agrees to distribute their apparels to Chinese e-commerce company <a href="/wiki/JD.com" title="JD.com">JD.com</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/18/jdcom-gap-idUSL3N0U238E20141218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A former US intelligence officer identifies Rolando "Rollie" Sarraff Trujillo as the Cuban Interior Ministry spy for the US <a href="/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" title="Central Intelligence Agency">Central Intelligence Agency</a>, who was swapped in exchange for members of the <a href="/wiki/Cuban_Five" title="Cuban Five">Cuban Five</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/investigations/cia-spy-sent-u-s-swap-identified-mole-cuban-interior-n271156" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_sanctions_during_the_2014_pro-Russian_unrest_in_Ukraine" title="International sanctions during the 2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine">International sanctions during the 2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> imposes sanctions on Russia-occupied <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimea</a> by banning investments and tourism in the region and halting oil explorations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/18/us-ukraine-crisis-eu-idUSKBN0JW18020141218" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Death_of_Jennifer_Laude" title="Death of Jennifer Laude">Death of Jennifer Laude</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> refuses to extradite a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Marine" title="United States Marine">United States Marine</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> where he is charged with <a href="/wiki/Murder" title="Murder">murder</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nydailynews.com/news/crime/embassy-not-hand-marine-filipino-courts-article-1.2048407" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Daily News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Death_Penalty_Information_Center" title="Death Penalty Information Center">Death Penalty Information Center</a> states that thirty-five people have been <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_the_United_States" title="Capital punishment in the United States">executed in the United States</a> in 2014, marking it the fewest number within two decades. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/nation/2014/12/17/executions-death-sentences-declining/20557375/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_District_of_South_Carolina" title="United States District Court for the District of South Carolina">US District Court for South Carolina</a> posthumously vacates the conviction of <a href="/wiki/George_Stinney" title="George Stinney">George Stinney, Jr.</a> seventy years after his execution. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/US/2014/12/17/George-Stinney-Jr-executed-at-14-cleared-of-murder-70-years-later/3251418842246/?r=2881418496650" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spanish_people" title="Spanish people">Spanish</a> police arrest thirteen more people, bringing the total now to more than seventy since the November 30th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Associated_football" title="Associated football">football</a> fan brawl, which resulted in one death, before the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atletico_Madrid" title="Atletico Madrid">Atletico Madrid</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Deportivo_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo La Coruña">Deportivo La Coruña</a> match started in Madrid's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vicente_Calderon_Stadium" title="Vicente Calderon Stadium">Vicente Calderon Stadium</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/sports/soccer/2014/12/18/spain-arrests-13-more-people-in-football-fan-fight/20576277/" rel="nofollow">(AP via USA Today)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indian_Space_Research_Organisation" title="Indian Space Research Organisation">India's</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Geosynchronous_Satellite_Launch_Vehicle_Mk_III" title="Geosynchronous Satellite Launch Vehicle Mk III">Geosynchronous Satellite Launch Vehicle Mk III</a> successfully completes its first flight, carrying the crew vehicle demonstrator <a href="/wiki/Crew_Module_Atmospheric_Re-entry_Experiment" title="Crew Module Atmospheric Re-entry Experiment">CARE</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/india/Isro-successfully-test-fires-GSLV-Mark-III-carrying-unmanned-crew-module/articleshow/45557579.cms" rel="nofollow"><i>(Times of India)</i></a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 19, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-19</span>)</span> (Friday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_19&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_19&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_19&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Armed_Forces" title="Pakistan Armed Forces">Pakistan Armed Forces</a> conduct operations in the <a href="/wiki/Federally_Administered_Tribal_Areas" title="Federally Administered Tribal Areas">Federally Administered Tribal Areas</a>, killing seventy-seven militants. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/news/crime/article/Pakistani-jets-ground-forces-kill-27-militants-5967588.php" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paramount_Pictures" title="Paramount Pictures">Paramount Pictures</a> orders theater chains, including those in <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">Cleveland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Atlanta" title="Atlanta">Atlanta</a>, and <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">New Orleans</a>, not to re-release the 2004 film <i><a href="/wiki/Team_America:_World_Police" title="Team America: World Police">Team America: World Police</a></i>, which depicts a fictional mission to kill <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.mercurynews.com/movies-dvd/ci_27159719/paramount-tells-theaters-no-team-america" rel="nofollow">(Mercury News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.nola.com/movies/index.ssf/2014/12/team_america_world_police_scre.html" rel="nofollow">(The Times-Picayune)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Staples_Inc." title="Staples Inc.">Staples</a> reports that 1.16 million customer <a href="/wiki/Credit_card" title="Credit card">payment cards</a> may have been affected in a data breach under investigation since October. <a class="external text" href="http://fortune.com/2014/12/19/staples-cards-affected-breach/" rel="nofollow">(Fortune)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A Vietnam official states that twelve <a href="/wiki/Vietnamese_people" title="Vietnamese people">Vietnamese</a> workers have been rescued three days after being trapped in a collapsed tunnel at a construction site of a hydropower plant located in <a href="/wiki/Central_Highlands_(Vietnam)" title="Central Highlands (Vietnam)">Central Highlands</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.salon.com/2014/12/19/12_workers_freed_from_collapsed_tunnel_in_vietnam/" rel="nofollow">(AP via Salon)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/19/us-vietnam-rescue-idUSKBN0JX1EV20141219" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> volcano <a href="/wiki/Gamalama" title="Gamalama">Gamalama</a> erupts injuring four people and leaving one person missing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.business-standard.com/article/pti-stories/indonesia-volcano-erupts-injuring-4-1-missing-114121900726_1.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Business Standard</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Centers_for_Disease_Control_and_Prevention" title="Centers for Disease Control and Prevention">Centers for Disease Control and Prevention</a> (CDC) links prepackaged <a href="/wiki/Caramel_apple" title="Caramel apple">caramel apples</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Listeria" title="Listeria">listeria</a> outbreak in ten US states that caused twenty-eight illnesses and four (or five) deaths. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/nation/2014/12/19/caramel-apples-listeria-outbreak/20636809/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Centers_for_Disease_Control_and_Prevention" title="Centers for Disease Control and Prevention">CDC</a> reports that for the US <a href="/wiki/Influenza" title="Influenza">flu</a> season cases are early and pervasive being widespread in 29 states, especially the South and Midwest. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/21a5c8debeaf44788361da7fa1fd4790/flu-season-early-again-hitting-hard-south-and-midwest" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_sanctions_during_the_2014_pro-Russian_unrest_in_Ukraine" title="International sanctions during the 2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine">International sanctions during the 2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine</a>
<ul>
<li>US President Barack Obama imposes additional sanctions on <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Crimea" title="Republic of Crimea">Russian-controlled Crimea</a> by an executive order forbidding exports of US goods and services to the region. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/business/international/us-slaps-trade-ban-on/1540372.html" rel="nofollow">(Channel NewsAsia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cairns_child_killings" title="Cairns child killings">Cairns child killings</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> police announce the finding that eight children were stabbed to death in a home in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cairns,_Australia" title="Cairns, Australia">Cairns</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/australia-news/2014/dec/19/at-least-seven-children-killed-in-mass-stabbing-in-cairns" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sun_Hung_Kai_Properties" title="Sun Hung Kai Properties">Sun Hung Kai Properties</a> Trial:
<ul>
<li>A Hong Kong jury convicts former <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> <a href="/wiki/Chief_Secretary_for_Administration" title="Chief Secretary for Administration">Chief Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Hui" title="Rafael Hui">Rafael Hui</a> of bribery charges in relation to <a href="/wiki/Malfeasance_in_office" title="Malfeasance in office">misconduct in office</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://rthk.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/news.htm?hightlight&amp;20141219&amp;56&amp;1062845" rel="nofollow">(RTHK English)</a></li>
<li>A Hong Kong jury acquits <a href="/wiki/Sun_Hung_Kai_Properties" title="Sun Hung Kai Properties">Sun Hung Kai Properties</a> Hong Kong tycoon <a href="/wiki/Raymond_Kwok" title="Raymond Kwok">Raymond Kwok</a> of all charges, while convicting his brother <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Kwok" title="Thomas Kwok">Thomas</a> of conspiracy to commit office misconduct. <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/2014/12/19/sunhungkai-trial-idINKBN0JX0JQ20141219" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://rthk.hk/rthk/news/englishnews/news.htm?hightlight&amp;20141219&amp;56&amp;1062845" rel="nofollow">(RTHK English)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/LGBT_rights_in_China" title="LGBT rights in China">LGBT rights in China</a>
<ul>
<li>In China, a court rules in favor of a gay man who sued a <a href="/wiki/Chongqing" title="Chongqing">Chongqing</a> <a href="/wiki/Electroconvulsive_therapy" title="Electroconvulsive therapy">electroconvulsive therapy</a> clinic that practises <a href="/wiki/Conversion_therapy" title="Conversion therapy">conversion therapy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2014/12/19/china-s-electroshock-gay-conversion-case.html" rel="nofollow">(The Daily Beast)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/South_Korean" title="South Korean">South Korean</a> court orders the dissolution of the <a href="/wiki/Unified_Progressive_Party" title="Unified Progressive Party">Unified Progressive Party</a> citing pro-<a href="/wiki/North_Korean" title="North Korean">North Korean</a> stances. <a class="external text" href="http://www.miamiherald.com/news/nation-world/article4651965.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Miami Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>Governor of <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">Vermont</a> <a href="/wiki/Peter_Shumlin" title="Peter Shumlin">Peter Shumlin</a> abandons plans for the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Single-payer_health_care" title="Single-payer health care">single-payer health care</a> system in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, citing transparency problems and heavy tax increases. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/blogs/govbeat/wp/2014/12/18/vermont-ends-push-for-single-payer-health-care/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Scientists withdraw the January 29, 2014 claim that there is a simple way to <a href="/wiki/Stimulus-triggered_acquisition_of_pluripotency" title="Stimulus-triggered acquisition of pluripotency">convert normal cells</a> into <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stem_cells" title="Stem cells">stem cells</a>, which can be used for any part of the body. <a href="/wiki/Nature_(journal)" title="Nature (journal)">Nature</a> had in July retracted its two previous articles after the disgraced lead researcher, Japanese <a href="/wiki/Haruko_Obokata" title="Haruko Obokata">Haruko Obokata</a>, was found to have plagiarized and fabricated parts of the papers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/health/2014/12/19/disgraced-japan-researcher-fails-to-replicate-game-changing-stem-cell-results" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_20&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Armed_Forces" title="Pakistan Armed Forces">Pakistan Armed Forces</a> attacks two <a href="/wiki/Tehrik-i-Taliban_Pakistan" title="Tehrik-i-Taliban Pakistan">Pakistani Taliban</a> positions near <a href="/wiki/Peshawar" title="Peshawar">Peshawar</a>, killing 5 militants. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30560482" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> launches an airstrike against an alleged <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> base near <a href="/wiki/Khan_Yunis" title="Khan Yunis">Khan Yunis</a> in retaliation for a rocket attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.com/2014/12/20/israel-launches-airstrike-on-gaza-in-apparent-retaliation-for-rocket-attack/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Arab-Israeli-Conflict/Gaza-rocket-lands-in-open-area-in-southern-Israel-no-injuries-385190" rel="nofollow">(The Jerusalem Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A bomb detonates in <a href="/wiki/Bani_Jamra" title="Bani Jamra">Bani Jamra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>, injuring 3 police officers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsj.com/articles/bahrain-blast-wounds-three-policemen-1419077098" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> government denies the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigations" title="Federal Bureau of Investigations">Federal Bureau of Investigations</a>'s (FBI) accusation of involvement in hacking Sony's computers, asking the U.S. for a joint investigation and threatening "serious consequences" if the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> refuses the offer of cooperation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessweek.com/news/2014-12-20/north-korea-seeks-joint-investigation-into-sony-hack-with-u-dot-s" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>The United States rejects the offer from North Korea and then seeks help <a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93North_Korea_relations" title="China–North Korea relations">from China</a> instead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/world/asia/la-fg-north-korea-proposes-joint-investigation-into-sony-hack-20141220-story.html" rel="nofollow">(LA Times)</a></li>
<li>Hackers send the FBI an email linking to a <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> video of "You are an idiot!" <a class="external text" href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2014/12/20/sony-hackers-guardians-of-peace-troll-fbi-fbi-is-the-best-in-the-world.html" rel="nofollow">(The Daily Beast)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.itv.com/news/2014-12-20/sony-hackers-mock-fbi-investigation-into-cyber-attack/" rel="nofollow">(ITV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> issues an arrest warrant for <a href="/wiki/Fethullah_G%C3%BClen" title="Fethullah Gülen">Fethullah Gülen</a>, who currently lives in self-imposed exile in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/12/20/world/europe/turkey-issues-arrest-warrant-for-a-rival-of-its-president.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cairns_child_killings" title="Cairns child killings">Cairns child killings</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> police arrest an Australian mother for murder in the stabbing deaths of eight children. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2014/12/20/8-children-killed-in-northern-australian-city/?intcmp=HPBucket" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_NYPD_officer_killings" title="2014 NYPD officer killings">2014 NYPD officer killings</a>
<ul>
<li>After shooting and wounding his ex-girlfriend in <a href="/wiki/Baltimore" title="Baltimore">Baltimore</a>, Ismaaiyl Brinsley shoots and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_NYPD_officer_killings" title="2014 NYPD officer killings">kills two policemen</a> <a href="/wiki/Execution-style_murder" title="Execution-style murder">execution style</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brooklyn" title="Brooklyn">Brooklyn</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a>, supposedly in revenge for the deaths of two black men in the U.S. reportedly caused by police officers during the summer of 2014, <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Eric_Garner" title="Death of Eric Garner">Eric Garner</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shooting_of_Michael_Brown" title="Shooting of Michael Brown">Michael Brown</a>. The gunman is later found dead of a self-inflicted gunshot wound in the <a href="/wiki/New_York_City_Subway" title="New York City Subway">subway</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/20/us/new-york-police-officers-shot/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a><a class="external text" href="http://baltimore.cbslocal.com/2014/12/20/baltimore-man-shoots-2-nypd-officer-1-dead-second-in-critical-condition/" rel="nofollow">(AP via CBS)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Hundreds of people from the group <a href="/wiki/Black_Lives_Matter" title="Black Lives Matter">Black Lives Matter</a> Minneapolis protest at the <a href="/wiki/Mall_of_America" title="Mall of America">Mall of America</a>, leading to its partial shutdown and 25 arrests. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/nation/2014/12/20/protesters-rally-at-mall-of-america/20698085/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In preparation for a government-proposed transportation tunnel, <a href="/wiki/Anthropologist" title="Anthropologist">anthropologists</a> discover 6,000-year-old <a href="/wiki/Charcoal" title="Charcoal">charcoal</a> at a site near <a href="/wiki/Stonehenge" title="Stonehenge">Stonehenge</a> suggesting an encampment existed much earlier than previously theorized. <a class="external text" href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2014/12/19/stonehenge-discovery-encampment_n_6355444.html" rel="nofollow">(Huffington Post)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/earth/environment/archaeology/11303127/Stonehenge-discovery-could-rewrite-British-pre-history.html" rel="nofollow">(The Telegraph)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.buckingham.ac.uk/latest-news/6000-year-old-encampment-found-in-dig-by-university-of-buckingham/" rel="nofollow">(University of Buckingham)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 21, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-21</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_21&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_21&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_21&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/British_people" title="British people">British</a> singer-songwriter <a href="/wiki/Elton_John" title="Elton John">Elton John</a> converts his <a href="/wiki/Domestic_partnership" title="Domestic partnership">domestic partnership</a> with filmmaker <a href="/wiki/David_Furnish" title="David Furnish">David Furnish</a> to <a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Same-sex marriage in the United Kingdom">marriage</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/entertainment/2014/12/21/elton-john-marries-longtime-partner-david-furnish-in-england/" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International Relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> temporarily reopens its <a href="/wiki/Gaza%E2%80%93Egypt_border" title="Gaza–Egypt border">border crossing</a> with <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza</a>, which had been closed since October, until 4 pm Monday. <a class="external text" href="http://english.ahram.org.eg/NewsContent/1/64/118496/Egypt/Politics-/Egypt-opens-Rafah-border-crossing-for-two-days.aspx" rel="nofollow">(Ahram Online)</a></li>
<li>Due to <a href="/wiki/Avian_influenza" title="Avian influenza">avian influenza</a> in the United States (<a href="/wiki/Oregon" title="Oregon">Oregon</a>), <a href="/wiki/South_Korea%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="South Korea–United States relations">South Korea suspends US imports</a> of poultry. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/business/international-business/South-Korea-halts-US-poultry-imports-due-to-bird-flu-in-US/articleshow/45592630.cms" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Times of India)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>After an eight-year informal <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Jordan" title="Capital punishment in Jordan">moratorium</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment" title="Capital punishment">death penalty</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a> executes 11 men. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/middleeast/2014/12/jordan-hangs-11-after-lifting-execution-ban-201412218257159168.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>China has detained more than thirty thousand people within two months for <a href="/wiki/Pornography_in_Asia#China" title="Pornography in Asia">pornography</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gambling_in_China" title="Gambling in China">gambling</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/22/us-china-internet-idUSKBN0K001720141222" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Beji_Caid_Essebsi" title="Beji Caid Essebsi">Beji Caid Essebsi</a> of the secularist <a href="/wiki/Nidaa_Tounes" title="Nidaa Tounes">Nidaa Tounes</a> party wins <a href="/wiki/Tunisian_presidential_election,_2014" title="Tunisian presidential election, 2014">Tunisia's presidential election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.alarabiya.net/en/News/middle-east/2014/12/21/Tunisians-vote-in-historic-presidential-run-off.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya English)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 22, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-22</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_22&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_22&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_22&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Peshawar_school_attack" title="2014 Peshawar school attack">2014 Peshawar school attack</a>
<ul>
<li>Following the December 17 announcement that it would lift its <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Pakistan" title="Capital punishment in Pakistan">moratorium</a> on terror-related <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment" title="Capital punishment">death penalty</a> cases, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> announces that it will execute 500 militants in the coming weeks. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/pakistan-plans-execute-500-terror-convicts-officials-093327925.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> experiences severe <a href="/wiki/Internet_in_North_Korea" title="Internet in North Korea">internet</a> outages. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/34ad411e0c9945a6a1d608ef54e988cf/north-korea-experiencing-severe-internet-outages" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>Bombings hit the <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigerian</a> cities of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gombe,_Nigeria" title="Gombe, Nigeria">Gombe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bauchi" title="Bauchi">Bauchi</a>, killing at least 26 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-30580578" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An out-of-control <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dustbin_lorry" title="Dustbin lorry">dustbin lorry</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Queen_Street,_Glasgow" title="Queen Street, Glasgow">Queen Street</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Square" title="George Square">George Square</a> areas of <a href="/wiki/Glasgow" title="Glasgow">Glasgow</a>, Scotland, kills at least six people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-scotland-glasgow-west-30580114" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_pro-Russian_unrest_in_Ukraine" title="2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine">2014 pro-Russian unrest in Ukraine</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a> renews its military cooperation with <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, to which it promises vital supplies of coal, following a visit to <a href="/wiki/Kiev" title="Kiev">Kiev</a> by the Kazakh leader, <a href="/wiki/Nursultan_Nazarbayev" title="Nursultan Nazarbayev">Nursultan Nazarbayev</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://latino.foxnews.com/latino/politics/2014/12/22/top-russian-allies-distance-themselves-from-putin-support-ukraine/" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_North_Korea" title="Human rights in North Korea">Human rights in North Korea</a>
<ul>
<li>Eleven (11) of 15 <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> members approve placing <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea's</a> <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> record on the Council's agenda. <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> and <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> oppose the decision while <a href="/wiki/Chad" title="Chad">Chad</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> abstain. This is the first time this issue has been debated by the Security Council. Procedurally, once a topic makes <a href="/wiki/Agenda_(meeting)" title="Agenda (meeting)">the agenda</a>, that issue can be brought up again at any time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessinsider.com/afp-china-fails-in-bid-to-block-un-meeting-on-n.-korea-2014-12" rel="nofollow">(Business Insider)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.chosun.com/site/data/html_dir/2014/12/24/2014122400608.html" rel="nofollow">(The Chosun Ilbo)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The US <a href="/wiki/Commodity_Futures_Trading_Commission" title="Commodity Futures Trading Commission">CFTC</a> fines <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Bank" title="Deutsche Bank">Deutsche Bank</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_dollars" title="United States dollars">$</a>3 million over customer fund flaws. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxbusiness.com/economy-policy/2014/12/22/us-cftc-fines-deutsche-bank-3b-over-customer-fund-flaws" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via FOX Business)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A federal land swap in <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a> green lights the US's deepest (1.3 miles) and largest (1.6b tons) copper mine. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/politics/2014/12/23/fed-land-swap-gives-go-ahead-to-arizona-16b-ton-copper-mega-mine/" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> December 23, 2014<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2014-12-23</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_23&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_23&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_23&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
