<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_Northeast_India" title="Insurgency in Northeast India">Insurgency in Northeast India</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_2014_Assam_violence" title="December 2014 Assam violence">December 2014 Assam violence</a>
<ul>
<li>Attacks on villages in the <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Assam" title="Assam">Assam</a> kill dozens of people. Suspicion falls on the insurgents of the <a href="/wiki/National_Democratic_Front_of_Bodoland" title="National Democratic Front of Bodoland">National Democratic Front of Bodoland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ndtv.com/article/india/43-people-killed-by-suspected-militants-assam-on-red-alert-638924" rel="nofollow">(NDTV)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.com/newswires/2856144-tribal-guerrillas-kill-33-in-wave-of-attacks-in-northeast-india/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/asia/2014/12/deaths-reported-northeast-india-attack-20141223151344571967.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>As a result, India imposes curfew on parts of Assam. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/india-imposes-curfew-after-attackers-kill-dozens-sectarian-violence-n274156" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Internet_in_North_Korea" title="Internet in North Korea">internet in North Korea</a> becomes functional again after nine hours without access. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2014/12/22/world/asia/north-korea-internet/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Korea_Hydro_%26_Nuclear_Power" title="Korea Hydro &amp; Nuclear Power">Korea Hydro &amp; Nuclear Power</a> says that its computer systems have been hacked. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/it-pro/security-it/south-korea-nuclear-plant-hacked-says-operator-20141222-12chrb.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>The death toll from the bombings in the <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigerian</a> cities of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gombe,_Nigeria" title="Gombe, Nigeria">Gombe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bauchi" title="Bauchi">Bauchi</a> reaches at least 37. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2014-12-23/nigerian-bombings-kill-at-least-27-in-two-northeastern-cities.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sony" title="Sony">Sony</a> schedules the film <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Interview_(2014_film)" title="The Interview (2014 film)">The Interview</a></i> for release to small theaters on Christmas Day despite canceling its debut. <a class="external text" href="http://jacksonville.com/breaking-news/2014-12-23/story/interview-will-be-debut-some-theaters-thursday-after-groundswell" rel="nofollow">(Florida Times-Union)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Businesses and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Keurig" title="Keurig">Keurig</a> recalls 6.6 million coffee making machines after ninety reports of burn-related injuries. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2014/12/23/news/companies/keurig-brewer-recall/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Tornado_outbreak" title="Tornado outbreak">tornado outbreak</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/December_2014_tornado_outbreak" title="December 2014 tornado outbreak">hits</a> the southern <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, producing five tornadoes with at least four people dead and leaving fifty others injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theweathernetwork.com/news/articles/deadly-tornado-outbreak-hits-the-us/42457/" rel="nofollow">(The Weather Network)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="Food and Drug Administration">FDA</a> says that in regards to the 31-year-old policy against gay men making blood donations it will recommend lifting the lifetime ban early next year, replacing it with a policy barring donations from men who have had sex with another man in the previous 12 months. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/c2680506d7a1448a928bf77ca4654a46/fda-ease-ban-blood-donations-gay-men" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The Parliament of <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> removes the country’s legislative block on forming military alliances, allowing the government to push forward with plans to accede to <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-30587924" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="Pakistan–Russia relations">Russia and Pakistan</a> sign their first energy deal for the <a href="/wiki/Karachi" title="Karachi">Karachi</a>–<a href="/wiki/Lahore" title="Lahore">Lahore</a> gas pipeline worth <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a>1.7 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://post.jagran.com/pakistan-russia-sign-usd-17billion-energy-deal-1419325505" rel="nofollow">(Jagran)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Hellenic_Parliament" title="Hellenic Parliament">Greek parliament</a> fails to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greek_presidential_election,_2014" title="Greek presidential election, 2014">elect a new president</a> in the second round of voting. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2014/dec/23/greece-presidential-vote-second-round" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iraqi_insurgency_(2011%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi insurgency (2011–present)">Iraqi insurgency</a>:
<ul>
<li>A suicide bombing in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Madaen" title="Madaen">Madaen</a> among a group of pro-government <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sunni" title="Sunni">Sunni</a> militiamen kills at least 33 people and leaves 55 others wounded. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/24/us-mideast-crisis-iraq-idUSKBN0K20GZ20141224" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/American-led_intervention_in_Syria" title="American-led intervention in Syria">American-led intervention in Syria</a>:
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Royal_Jordanian_Air_Force" title="Royal Jordanian Air Force">Royal Jordanian Air Force</a> warplane crashes, and its pilot is captured by <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> militants near the city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ar-Raqqah" title="Ar-Raqqah">Ar-Raqqah</a> in northern <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-30596474" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li>Sony releases the film <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Interview_(2014_film)" title="The Interview (2014 film)">The Interview</a></i> online via <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">YouTube</a> and <a href="/wiki/Google_Play" title="Google Play">Google Play</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/24/us-northkorea-cybersecurity-youtube-idUSKBN0K210520141224" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Russia declares a state of emergency after oil from a Russian oil pipeline spills into the <a href="/wiki/Black_Sea" title="Black Sea">Black Sea</a> near the port of <a href="/wiki/Tuapse" title="Tuapse">Tuapse</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/24/us-russia-oil-spill-idUSKBN0K20ND20141224" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93South_Korea_relations" title="China–South Korea relations">South Korea seeks China</a>'s investigational assistance concerning the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Korea_Hydro_and_Nuclear_Power" title="Korea Hydro and Nuclear Power">Korea Hydro and Nuclear Power</a> hackings. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/24/us-northkorea-cybersecurity-nuclear-idUSKBN0K20DT20141224?feedType=RSS" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><i>Xinhua</i> reports that on December 21 Chinese police in <a href="/wiki/Guangxi" title="Guangxi">Guangxi</a> shot dead one person and detained 21 others. China considers the group to be "religious extremists" who were trying to cross the border into <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/24/us-china-thailand-idUSKBN0K204720141224" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_25&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<ul>

</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2009%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2009–present)">Somali civil war</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al-Shabab</a> militants attack <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AMISOM" title="AMISOM">AMISOM</a>'s headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>, leaving three peacekeeping soldiers and a civilian contractor dead. Five of the attackers are also killed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/africa/2014/12/reports-al-shabab-strikes-au-base-somalia-20141225112253311677.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Army_of_Pakistan" title="Army of Pakistan">Pakistani forces</a> report the killing of the "mastermind" behind the <a href="/wiki/2014_Peshawar_school_massacre" title="2014 Peshawar school massacre">Peshawar school massacre</a> during a gun battle in the <a href="/wiki/Khyber_Agency" title="Khyber Agency">Khyber Agency</a> <a href="/wiki/Federally_Administered_Tribal_Areas" title="Federally Administered Tribal Areas">tribal area</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/asia/pakistan/11313678/Mastermind-of-Peshawar-school-attack-killed.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Ebola_epidemic" title="2014 Ebola epidemic">2014 Ebola epidemic</a>

<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> praises <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces">U.S. troops</a> and reflects on the <a href="/wiki/Withdrawal_of_U.S._troops_from_Afghanistan" title="Withdrawal of U.S. troops from Afghanistan">U.S. withdrawal</a> from <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> during his annual Christmas message from <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">Hawaii</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com/news/world/2014/12/25/president_obama_reflects_on_afghanistan_mission_in_christmas_address.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Toronto Star</i>)</a></li>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2014_December_26&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> and <a href="/wiki/Donetsk_People%27s_Republic" title="Donetsk People's Republic">pro-Russia rebels</a> exchange nearly 370 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prisoners_of_war" title="Prisoners of war">prisoners</a> in the largest such exchange since hostilities began in April this year. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/talks-ukraine-settlement-break-27835215" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> and the local <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_the_Philippines" title="Communist Party of the Philippines">Communist Party</a> agree to renew talks that may lead to a <a href="/wiki/Peace_treaty" title="Peace treaty">peace treaty</a> which could end the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CPP-NPA-NDF_rebellion" title="CPP-NPA-NDF rebellion">46-year communist insurgency</a> in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/mobile/asiapacific/peace-talks-with/1550294.html" rel="nofollow">(Channel News Asia)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-2887400/Philippine-communist-rebels-say-peace-talks-resume-soon.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>

<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Southeast_Asian_floods" title="2014 Southeast Asian floods">2014 Southeast Asian floods</a>
<ul>
<li>Flooding in <a href="/wiki/Peninsular_Malaysia" title="Peninsular Malaysia">Peninsular Malaysia</a> forces the evacuation of over 100,000 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.worldbulletin.net/news/151652/103000-evacuated-in-record-breaking-malaysia-floods" rel="nofollow">(World Bulletin)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>Countries around the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a> commemorate the tenth anniversary of the tsunami. <a class="external text" href="http://m.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30602159" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Three South Korean workers die at a nuclear plant construction site. There is speculation that the deaths are connected to a <a href="/wiki/Korea_Hydro_%26_Nuclear_Power" title="Korea Hydro &amp; Nuclear Power">recent nuclear power plant attack</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2014/12/26/3-s-korean-workers-die-after-apparently-inhaling-toxic-gas-at-nuclear-plant/" rel="nofollow">(AP via FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The Special Investigation Division of <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> initiates a review stemming from allegations that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Taiwan" title="President of Taiwan">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Ma_Ying-jeou" title="Ma Ying-jeou">Ma Ying-jeou</a> has received illegal political donations from <a href="/wiki/Ting_Hsin_International_Group" title="Ting Hsin International Group">Ting Hsin International Group</a>, a disgraced conglomerate at the center of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Taiwan_food_scandal" title="2014 Taiwan food scandal">recent food scandal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://focustaiwan.cna.com.tw/news/aipl/201412250028.aspx" rel="nofollow">(Central News Agency)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures_Entertainment_hack" title="Sony Pictures Entertainment hack">Sony Pictures Entertainment hack</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>'s embassy in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> issues a statement, saying: "The film <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Interview_(2014_film)" title="The Interview (2014 film)">The Interview</a></i>, produced by the U.S. studio <a href="/wiki/Sony_Pictures" title="Sony Pictures">Sony Pictures</a>, is a very dangerous film product that justifies and promotes terrorism." <a class="external text" href="http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/russian-official-speaks-interview-release-760370" rel="nofollow">(<i>Hollywood Reporter</i>)</a></li>
<li>Russian Foreign Ministry’s official spokesman Alexander Lukashevich says that "the mere idea of the film is aggressively scandalous and that the reaction of the North Korean side is very understandable." <a class="external text" href="http://itar-tass.com/en/russia/769186" rel="nofollow">(TASS)</a></li>
<li>A report says that even before the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> Christmas Eve release of <i>The Interview</i>, thousands of Chinese citizens were downloading pirated versions of the movie on domestic video-sharing websites. By midday on December 26, more than 300,000 people had seen the film. <a class="external text" href="http://sinosphere.blogs.nytimes.com/2014/12/26/chinese-viewers-mostly-give-thumbs-up-for-the-interview/?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(The New York Times)</a></li>
<li><i>The Interview</i> grosses US$1 million on Christmas Day at the box office despite being released only to small theaters. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2014/12/26/media/the-interview-box-office-results/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Hackers cause the <a href="/wiki/PlayStation_Network" title="PlayStation Network">PlayStation Network</a> and <a href="/wiki/Xbox_Live" title="Xbox Live">Xbox Live</a> to suffer connection difficulties on Christmas Day. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/tech/gaming/2014/12/25/xbox-live-playstation-network-hack/20895113/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Cricket" title="Cricket">cricket</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Boxing_Day_Test" title="Boxing Day Test">Boxing Day Test</a> commences at the <a href="/wiki/Melbourne_Cricket_Ground" title="Melbourne Cricket Ground">Melbourne Cricket Ground</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_cricket_team" title="Australia national cricket team">Australia</a> playing against <a href="/wiki/India_national_cricket_team" title="India national cricket team">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/sport/cricket/boxing-day-test-2014-ryan-harris-back-as-aussies-relish-indians-whingeing-20141225-12dmfq.html" rel="nofollow">(The Sydney Morning Herald)</a></li>
</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/Andrei_Kobyakov" title="Andrei Kobyakov">Andrei Kobyakov</a> replaces <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Myasnikovich" title="Mikhail Myasnikovich">Mikhail Myasnikovich</a> as <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a>'s new prime minister in the biggest government reshuffle since 2010. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/lukashenka-belarus-new-prime-minister/26765257.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2001–present)">War in Afghanistan</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Security_Assistance_Force" title="International Security Assistance Force">International Security Assistance Force</a> formally ends its combat mission. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/28/us-afghanistan-war-idUSKBN0K60FB20141228" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indonesia_AirAsia_Flight_8501" title="Indonesia AirAsia Flight 8501">Indonesia AirAsia Flight 8501</a>
<ul>
<li>Traveling through thunderstorms over the <a href="/wiki/Java_Sea" title="Java Sea">Java Sea</a>, Flight 8501 loses contact with air traffic control after the plane departed from the <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Surabaya" title="Surabaya">Surabaya</a> en route to <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a> with 162 people on board. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-30614627" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The Italian-owned <a href="/wiki/MS_Norman_Atlantic" title="MS Norman Atlantic">MS <i>Norman Atlantic</i></a> catches fire on a ferry run from <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> to <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> 44 nautical miles northwest of <a href="/wiki/Corfu" title="Corfu">Corfu</a>, with 222 vehicles, 411 passengers and 5 crew on board. Greek and Italian officials report at least one person is dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/norman-atlantic-ablaze-major-rescue-under-way-as-greeceitaly-ferry-evacuated-in-high-winds-9946679.html" rel="nofollow">(The Independent)</a>,<a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-30615721" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Two merchant ships collide in rough seas off the <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> <a href="/wiki/Adriatic_Sea" title="Adriatic Sea">Adriatic coast</a>, leaving at least one person dead and two missing. <a class="external text" href="http://news24.com/news24/World/News/Two-merchant-ships-collide-off-Italy-20141228" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via News24)</a></li>
<li>Floods and mudslides in <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a> kill at least twenty-four people and leave eight missing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.japantimes.co.jp/life/2014/12/28/environment/floods-mudslides-sri-lanka-leave-24-dead-eight-missing/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Japan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>An apartment building fire near <a href="/wiki/San_Antonio" title="San Antonio">San Antonio</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, USA, kills five people. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/37b68da3cfc74f7ca854e3f875049404/5-dead-apartment-building-fire-near-san-antonio" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Croatian_presidential_election,_2014" title="Croatian presidential election, 2014">Croatian presidential election</a> goes to a run-off between incumbent <a href="/wiki/Ivo_Josipovi%C4%87" title="Ivo Josipović">Ivo Josipović</a> and challenger <a href="/wiki/Kolinda_Grabar-Kitarovi%C4%87" title="Kolinda Grabar-Kitarović">Kolinda Grabar-Kitarović</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/2014-12-27/croats-head-to-polls-as-president-vies-for-re-election.html" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<ul>
<li>In the latest advance in <a href="/wiki/Operation_Indian_Ocean" title="Operation Indian Ocean">Operation Indian Ocean</a>, Somali government forces assisted by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AMISOM" title="AMISOM">AMISOM</a> troops capture seven towns in the central <a href="/wiki/Hiran,_Somalia" title="Hiran, Somalia">Hiran</a> province from <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al-Shabaab</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.garoweonline.com/page/show/post/1343/somalia-federal-govt-au-forces-liberate-new-areas-in-hiran" rel="nofollow">(Garowe Online)</a></li>

</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cameroonian_Armed_Forces" title="Cameroonian Armed Forces">Cameroon</a> launches its first airstrikes against Boko Haram in a successful operation to reclaim several villages and a military base <a href="/wiki/December_2014_Cameroon_clashes" title="December 2014 Cameroon clashes">briefly seized</a> by the militant group in the <a href="/wiki/Far_North_Region_(Cameroon)" title="Far North Region (Cameroon)">Far North Region</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-30623199" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/MS_Norman_Atlantic" title="MS Norman Atlantic">MS <i>Norman Atlantic</i></a> ferry fire death toll rises to at least ten as the evacuation ends. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-30624086" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ebola_virus_epidemic_in_West_Africa" title="Ebola virus epidemic in West Africa">Ebola outbreak</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Glasgow" title="Glasgow">Glasgow</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gartnavel_General_Hospital" title="Gartnavel General Hospital">Gartnavel Hospital</a> diagnoses a woman, who arrived from <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a>, as the first case of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ebola" title="Ebola">Ebola</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">UK</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/uk-scotland-30628349" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A fire in a <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> shopping mall kills at least 13 people. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/9a185b19bc524afcb1f6099233813c62/fire-pakistan-shopping-mall-reportedly-kills-least-13" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Greek_legislative_election,_January_2015" title="Greek legislative election, January 2015">Snap elections</a> are to be called after the <a href="/wiki/Hellenic_Parliament" title="Hellenic Parliament">Hellenic Parliament</a> fails to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Greek_presidential_election,_2014" title="Greek presidential election, 2014">elect a new Greek president</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/29/us-greece-vote-idUSKBN0K60MA20141229" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The Chinese government <a href="/wiki/Internet_in_China" title="Internet in China">blocks</a> some of <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gmail" title="Gmail">Gmail</a> services. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/29/us-google-china-idUSKBN0K70BD20141229" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>A US airstrike in <a href="/wiki/Saakow" title="Saakow">Saakow</a> kills the intelligence chief, Abdishakur, who was also known as Tahlil, of the <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somali</a> <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabab</a> militants. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/a355b3195cfd404081474f8c18f07b14/somalia-says-us-airstrike-kills-al-shabab-leader" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>

<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Luise_Rainer" title="Luise Rainer">Luise Rainer</a>, German-born American actress (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Great_Ziegfeld" title="The Great Ziegfeld">The Great Ziegfeld</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Good_Earth_(film)" title="The Good Earth (film)">The Good Earth</a></i>), <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress" title="Academy Award for Best Actress">Academy Award</a> winner (<a href="/wiki/9th_Academy_Awards" title="9th Academy Awards">1936</a>, <a href="/wiki/10th_Academy_Awards" title="10th Academy Awards">1937</a>), dies of pneumonia at the age of 104. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/entertainment-arts-30631088" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>

<ul>

</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014_Southeast_Asian_floods" title="2014 Southeast Asian floods">2014 Southeast Asian floods</a>
<ul>
<li>Flooding and the death toll continues in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/30/southeast-asia-floods-idUSL3N0UE2IB20141230" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>

<li>In three separate, but connected, crime scenes in <a href="/wiki/Edmonton" title="Edmonton">Edmonton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alberta" title="Alberta">Alberta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, a suicidal man <a href="/wiki/2014_Edmonton_killings" title="2014 Edmonton killings">kills</a> eight people and then himself. <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/news/world/us/nine-dead-in-edmonton-canada-shooting-incidents-1.2051535" rel="nofollow"><i>(Irish Times)</i></a></li>

<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/2014_Ibb_bombing" title="2014 Ibb bombing">suicide bombing</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ibb" title="Ibb">Ibb</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>, kills at least 26 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/31/us-yemen-attack-idUSKBN0K90JK20141231" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">United States stock exchange</a> reports ending on a gain of 7.5%. It was the sixth year of continued advancement. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsj.com/articles/u-s-stock-futures-edge-upward-1420032056" rel="nofollow">(Wall Street Journal)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2014_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2014 Pacific typhoon season">Pacific typhoon season</a>
<ul>
<li>As <a href="/wiki/2014_Pacific_typhoon_season#Tropical_Storm_Jangmi_.28Seniang.29" title="2014 Pacific typhoon season">Tropical Storm Jangmi (Seniang)</a> weakens, the Philippines death toll reaches 53 people. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/dc32aa3e21ac4e1885ba93eb12efe339/philippine-storm-weakens-leaves-53-dead" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Explosions at a factory in the southern Chinese city of <a href="/wiki/Foshan" title="Foshan">Foshan</a> kill 17 people and injure 20. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/12/31/us-china-blast-punishment-idUSKBN0K903520141231" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A New Year's Eve celebration <a href="/wiki/2014_Shanghai_stampede" title="2014 Shanghai stampede">stampede</a> in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a> kills at least 36 people and injures 49 others. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-china-30646918" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/china/2015-01/02/content_19222400.htm" rel="nofollow">(China Daily)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Corps_of_the_Port_Captaincies_%E2%80%93_Coast_Guard" title="Corps of the Port Captaincies – Coast Guard">Italian coast guard</a> boards and regains control of a <a href="/wiki/Cargo_ship" title="Cargo ship">cargo ship</a> that had been sabotaged and abandoned by human traffickers carrying nearly 1,000 passengers, mostly <a href="/wiki/Refugees_of_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Refugees of the Syrian Civil War">Syrian refugees</a>, that was in imminent jeopardy of crashing into land. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsj.com/articles/italian-coast-guard-steers-ship-with-hundreds-of-migrants-aboard-away-from-collision-course-1420028650" rel="nofollow">(Wall Street Journal)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.enca.com/world/disaster-avoided-runaway-ship-stopped-italy-900-aboard" rel="nofollow">(eNews Channel Africa)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Riot" title="Riot">riot</a> breaks out at a New Year's Eve festival in <a href="/wiki/Gisborne,_New_Zealand" title="Gisborne, New Zealand">Gisborne</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, leaving 83 people injured and 63 arrested. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=11380838" rel="nofollow">(NZ Herald)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Italy" title="President of Italy">President of Italy</a> <a href="/wiki/Giorgio_Napolitano" title="Giorgio Napolitano">Giorgio Napolitano</a> announces his impending resignation, citing "old age". <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessweek.com/news/2014-12-31/italian-president-to-resign-posing-challenge-for-renzi" rel="nofollow">(Business Week)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Gambia" title="President of Gambia">President of Gambia</a> <a href="/wiki/Yahya_Jammeh" title="Yahya Jammeh">Yahya Jammeh</a> remains in power after a <a href="/wiki/2014_Gambian_coup_d%27%C3%A9tat_attempt" title="2014 Gambian coup d'état attempt">failed coup attempt</a> while he was travelling outside the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/africa/2014/12/gambia-leader-return-after-coup-attempt-2014123191702890.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nur_Bekri" title="Nur Bekri">Nur Bekri</a> resigns as the Chairman of the <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a> Uyghur Autonomous Region of China to become the Director of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Energy_Administration" title="National Energy Administration">National Energy Administration</a>, and is replaced in the interim by <a href="/wiki/Shohrat_Zakir" title="Shohrat Zakir">Shohrat Zakir</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.business-standard.com/article/pti-stories/china-shifts-top-uygur-official-from-xinjiang-114123100762_1.html" rel="nofollow">(Business Standard)</a></li>
<li>China relieves <a href="/wiki/Sun_Chunlan" title="Sun Chunlan">Sun Chunlan</a> of her post as <a href="/wiki/Party_Committee_Secretary" title="Party Committee Secretary">Party Committee Secretary</a> of <a href="/wiki/Tianjin" title="Tianjin">Tianjin</a>, China, and replaces her on an interim basis with <a href="/wiki/Huang_Xingguo" title="Huang Xingguo">Huang Xingguo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.scmp.com/news/china/article/1671585/confusion-rare-multiple-reshuffle" rel="nofollow">(SCMP)</a></li>
<li>As part of an agreement with <a href="/wiki/Djibouti" title="Djibouti">Djibouti</a>'s Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Abdoulkader_Kamil_Mohamed" title="Abdoulkader Kamil Mohamed">Abdoulkader Kamil</a>, the country's main opposition party, the <a href="/wiki/Union_for_National_Salvation" title="Union for National Salvation">Union for National Salvation</a>, decides to return to its eight seats in the National Assembly after having boycotted it since the <a href="/wiki/Djiboutian_parliamentary_election,_2013" title="Djiboutian parliamentary election, 2013">parliamentary election in 2013</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw.de/djibouti-government-makes-deal-with-opposition/a-18165740" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
